Current Commentary

Another Opinion on Preventing the Outflow of Silver

— Yin Pu

│ Advocating "Blocking Silver from Flowing into Foreign Banks"

Since the United States adopted a policy of raising silver prices to purchase silver, world silver prices have become increasingly strong. As a result, China's silver has experienced a huge outflow. The result of artificially raising the price of silver is that, at the same time, its overseas rise is often higher than domestic. In other words, in the process of silver price increases, overseas silver prices are often slightly more expensive than domestic silver prices. At this time, it is quite profitable to transport cheaper domestic silver abroad for sale. According to recent information (late August, 1934), exporting silver can yield a net profit of 4% to 5% after deducting all expenses such as transportation, insurance, wooden box costs, and smelting losses. (That is, every million yuan of silver exported can generate about 40,000 to 50,000 yuan in profit.) Statistics show that this year (as of August 24), the total amount of silver exported from Shanghai has reached a huge 111.5 million yuan in national currency. This export of silver has accounted for more than half of the total in the last two months. The number of exports from other ports, such as Xiamen, is not included. In a very short period of time, such a large amount of silver was exported, which can be generally seen as speculative profit-seeking rather than offsetting international payments.

In recent years, due to the bankruptcy of rural areas in the interior of China, domestic silver has been concentrated in urban areas, and there is already a phenomenon of silver depletion in the interior. If urban silver continues to flow out of the country, then cities in the interior will also feel the lack of silver, and the financial system built on the foundation of silver will inevitably encounter difficulties first. The outflow of silver reduces the silver base, which restricts the issuance reserve. In a situation where hard currency is already scarce, the inability to increase paper currency further exacerbates the situation. As a result, currency is insufficient, and credit is contracted. On the one hand, due to financial tension, the domestic liquidity is less smooth; on the other hand, the resulting decline in prices and exchange rates will inevitably lead to industrial decline and foreign goods flooding the market. The entire national economy will therefore fall into a desperate situation. Therefore, contemporary scholars have proposed many measures to prevent the outflow of silver. However, because of different perspectives, it is difficult to reach a consensus.

In my humble opinion, all parties seem to have fundamental errors in observation and concepts. As a result, the conclusions reached are inevitably unrealistic and not thorough. What are the errors in observation? It lies in combining the silver reserves of the domestic financial sector with the silver reserves of foreign banks without distinction. What are the errors in concept? It lies in only seeking to prevent the outflow of silver without also seeking to avoid the adverse effects of rising silver prices.

First, let me state the facts regarding the first point: although foreign banks and the domestic financial sector seem to have mutual transactions in normal exchanges, in reality, they have long been divided. All daily payments, except for offsetting with clearinghouse bills, must be settled in cash. If a large amount of deposits from Chinese people are transferred to foreign banks today, then the settlement result today is that some silver must flow into foreign banks. If a large amount of foreign goods arrive at the port tomorrow, and the price must be paid, then the settlement result tomorrow is that some silver must flow into foreign banks again. After this large amount of silver flows into foreign banks, it is completely separated from the domestic financial market. From then on, no matter how tight the domestic financial market is or how urgent the need for silver is, this silver that has already entered foreign banks is "once inside the noble's door," and they are indifferent to the pain. Those who enter American banks are now American silver; those who enter British banks are now British silver; those who enter the banks of Germany, France, and other countries are now the silver of Germany, France, and other countries. Sovereignty belongs to others, and we cannot intervene in their comings and goings. Therefore, I believe that it is good for foreign banks to keep silver in Shanghai, and it is also good for them to leave Shanghai. Those who stay keep their form. In substance and effect, they have already left the country by thousands of miles and are roaming in the cities of London and New York. Since we cannot steal and seize them and take them as our own, what good does it do us to keep this silver carcass on our land? Those who talk about preventing the outflow of silver today are ignorant of this point. Therefore, if we talk about imposing silver taxes, they are afraid that foreign banks will transport and store them in Hong Kong and wait for an opportunity. If we talk about banning silver exports, they worry that foreign banks will sell them to the government and temporarily store them overseas. Some even advocate contacting the US government to purchase silver in Shanghai. As if the silver purchased by the US government in Shanghai is still ours. I ask, what is the difference in substance and effect between temporarily storing US silver in Shanghai and transporting US silver to New York? This fundamental error in the observation of all parties should be explained first.

The impact of rising silver prices is that domestic prices fall and foreign exchange rates fall (meaning that each unit of domestic currency can buy more foreign currency). Falling prices spread the recession throughout the country. The already bankrupt agriculture has no hope of revival. The declining industry is even more in danger of collapse. Falling exchange rates reduce the price of foreign goods and increase the price of domestic goods. The country is flooded with foreign goods, and domestic goods are unsalable abroad. As a result, the national economy is in a state of internal and external difficulties and declines day by day. Therefore, the countermeasure to prevent the outflow of silver should include the effect of suppressing domestic silver prices. Otherwise, if foreign silver rises, we will use manpower to raise domestic silver prices to keep pace with it. Under this situation, domestic and foreign silver prices form a straight line. The outflow of silver may be prevented, but it will help the wave of rising silver prices and stand up to the adverse effects of this silver rise. What is that for? This fundamental error in the concept of the commentators should be explained first.

So, what is the strategy to prevent the outflow of silver while avoiding the impact of rising silver prices? There is only one method: "blocking silver from flowing into foreign banks."

The simplest, easiest to implement, and effective method to "block silver from flowing into foreign banks" is only the method of "no cash withdrawals for remittances and transfers." In extraordinary times, extraordinary methods should be used. "No cash withdrawals for remittances and transfers" is different from and actually the same as stopping the silver standard in its application. Stopping the silver standard internationally becomes a "paper currency standard"; "no cash withdrawals for remittances and transfers" becomes a "clearing account standard" or a "bill standard" internationally. In fact, it is not easy or possible to stop the silver standard in our country today. Because the power of issuance in our country has not yet been centralized, it is impossible to compile paper currency. It is also difficult to achieve centralization in a short time in reality. Therefore, it seems easier to promote "no cash withdrawals for remittances and transfers" to avoid difficulties. However, under the "clearing account standard" or "bill standard," there is one point that must be noted internally: that is, there should be a considerable restriction on withdrawing deposits or redeeming banknotes. Otherwise, if cash withdrawals of deposits or banknote redemptions can obtain unlimited cash, there is still a chance for cash to flow into foreign banks, and I am afraid it will still be of no practical help. Therefore, before implementing "no cash withdrawals for remittances and transfers," it seems that the registration of silver reserves of each domestic bank should be done first, and a public announcement should be made to gain the trust of the people. At the same time, for withdrawals (cash withdrawals can be unlimited) and redemptions, a considerable restriction should be set for those who want to withdraw cash. In this way, with decentralized reserves, it has the effect of centralization. Why can't it achieve the goal of "blocking silver from flowing into foreign banks"?

"No cash withdrawals for remittances and transfers" can "block silver from flowing into foreign banks"; "blocking silver from flowing into foreign banks" is equivalent to stopping the silver standard; stopping the silver standard can separate the domestic currency value from foreign silver prices; separating the domestic currency value from foreign silver prices can avoid the adverse effects of foreign silver price increases.

Therefore, I say that to prevent the outflow of silver while avoiding the impact of rising silver prices, there is only one method: "blocking silver from flowing into foreign banks"; that is, there is only one method: "no cash withdrawals for remittances and transfers."

Editor's Note: Since the United States raised silver prices, China's silver has surged out, causing a major panic in the domestic silver market. In view of the continued massive outflow of silver, the banking sector and economists in this city have discussed countermeasures to prevent it. However, since this matter is complex, commentators have different opinions. For example, the article by Mr. Yin Pu above and the article by Mr. Ci Xing, "Effective Measures to Prevent the Outflow of Silver," published in this column yesterday, have quite different arguments, but each has its own unique insights. Because many people in the country are paying attention to this issue, we have specifically disclosed them one after another for comparison and reference.

International Currency War

Rumors of Britain's Plan to Restore the Gold Standard

Pound Depreciation is a Retaliation Against the United States

The United States Declares No Change in Gold Policy

(London) The international currency war has broken out in all directions. There are significant signs of this in London today. France and Switzerland purchased many francs today. Furthermore, according to reliable information, the British Equalization Fund has also moved this afternoon, selling approximately one million pounds of gold. Gold prices soared, and the pound plummeted. Experts believe that this is Britain's retaliatory action against the US's nationalization of silver and the resulting depreciation of the dollar. It is said that the pound's depreciation will prompt President Roosevelt to devalue the dollar again. London's gold prices soared today. An ounce of pure gold soared by 7.5 pence, reaching 131 shillings and 3 pence. (24th, Guomin News Agency)

(Washington) Treasury experts are now closely monitoring foreign exchange rumors and their impact on the dollar, but believe that the talk of a currency war with Britain is unfounded. (24th, Guomin News Agency)

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau announced today that the Treasury Department's policy of allowing free export of cash has not changed. Mr. Morgenthau also said that if the dollar depreciates to the point where it is profitable to sell cash at $35 per ounce, the Treasury Department is ready to sell cash at any time. Mr. Morgenthau's declaration was issued due to rumors in New York, Paris, and other financial markets that the United States plans to devalue the dollar again. The Secretary of the Treasury also said that he is not worried about the current foreign exchange situation and does not know why people in the general banking and financial sectors are so gullible. (23rd, Guomin News Agency)

(New York) All financial centers around the world today are rife with rumors about currency issues. One says that Britain plans to restore the gold standard, so the British Exchange Equalization Fund has stopped supporting the pound's exchange rate against the franc. However, the pound's depreciation does not seem likely to materialize, because insurance companies are still charging a premium of one in a thousand for insurance against the government confiscating cash or restoring the gold standard by depreciating the pound. Therefore, the British government will probably not nationalize cash or lower the price of the pound. As for the United States, according to reliable sources, the Treasury Department does not intend to reduce the gold content of the dollar to below 59.6 cents. Generally speaking, the US government's currency policy will not change before the end of this year. Financial experts believe that if the dollar is lowered now, the huge amount of money needed by the government next month will greatly affect the treasury. Economic circles here say that a large amount of cash can now be transported abroad to maintain the dollar, while the domestic situation can still be unaffected. There have already been several batches of cash exports. According to dispatches from Paris, the pound has fallen to 76.3 francs since the British Exchange Equalization Fund stopped supporting the pound. French economists predict that London will further suppress the pound's price. If so, the world will implement a currency war. Silver continues to be shipped from Britain to the United States. Since the United States nationalized silver, Britain has shipped 1,000 tons of silver to the United States. (23rd, Guomin News Agency)

British Silver Shipped to the United States Reaches 1,000 Tons

(London) The American ship President Harding is scheduled to load silver worth 1.25 million pounds tomorrow and depart from Southampton, England, for New York. This is a new record for silver being shipped from Britain to the United States, with a total of 12,134 bars, which is nine more than the amount shipped on the Washington last week. This silver was transferred from London to the port of Southampton in 50 railway freight cars, weighing about 400 tons. Including this time, the silver shipped to the United States in the past half month is almost 1,000 tons. (23rd, Reuters)

Large Amount of American Gold Shipped to France

(New York) It was learned today that the Manhattan Bank will ship gold worth 1.5 million yuan to Paris on August 25. This shipment was expected, because the value of foreign currencies has been strong recently, especially the franc. (23rd, Reuters)

Mussolini

Looking down on Central Europe

Delivers a major post-exercise declaration to foreign countries

The rise and fall of a nation depends on military strength

Italy is always prepared for war

(Bologna) After the conclusion of the Italian army's major exercise, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini addressed foreign military delegations today, stating that no one desires war, but war can break out at any moment. We must be prepared for war; we must not wait until tomorrow but plan for today. The situation that occurred at the end of July reminded people of the situation in 1914. We immediately stationed troops on the border, which preserved the overall situation. We must train our people not to forget military affairs and to be a people united against the enemy. The rise and fall of a nation depend on military strength. All Italians must dedicate themselves to the battlefield in the event of war. The Prime Minister also stated that the terrain where this major exercise took place is very similar to Italy's eastern border. The Prime Minister's remarks are highly valued, as Italy recently sent troops to the Austrian border, and military delegations from Germany and Yugoslavia were present to observe the exercise. (Reuters, 24th)

Austrian Chancellor Returns to Vienna

What mission did he have in France?

No way to find out the truth

Someone saw him sunbathing on the beach

(Nice, France) Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg, who came here for rest, has now departed for Vienna. (Havas, 24th)

(Paris) The sudden arrival of Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg in Nice, France, has greatly surprised the French general public. Everyone wants to know what mission the Austrian Chancellor has here. If he only claims to be here for a short rest, it is hardly believable. Therefore, reporters from various newspapers automatically organized a guard this morning at 10:00 AM, surrounding the hotel where the Austrian Chancellor was staying. However, they were ultimately disappointed because the Austrian Chancellor had already left early in the morning in his secretary's car, and his destination was unknown. It was later discovered that the car carrying the Austrian Chancellor and his secretary was found on the beach in Grasse. It is said that the two spent the whole day lying on the beach sunbathing. As for the reports in various newspapers yesterday that the Austrian Chancellor would be talking with officials from France, Britain, and Romania, this has not yet been confirmed. The Paris Evening News sent a reporter to Èze to interview British Deputy Prime Minister Baldwin to inquire whether he would meet with the Austrian Chancellor. The Berlin Daily News stated that requesting Germany to guarantee Austria's independence may not ease the relationship between Germany and Austria. This move is merely a means, and its intention is elsewhere. (Havas, 24th)

Grand opening in Nuremberg at the beginning of next month

Hitler

Rounding up dissidents in one fell swoop

Says it has nothing to do with voting

Four hundred political prisoners granted amnesty

(Berlin) Foreign newspapers claim that the National Socialist Party has begun punishing those who voted against Hitler on August 19. The German News Agency issued a press release denying this, stating, "It is rumored that the German government will severely punish people who voted against it in the previous election, and the recent arrest of 150 people is the beginning of this action. Many foreign newspapers have published such news. According to foreign reports, most of those arrested are Catholics and Jews, who regard this as the beginning of the exclusion and abuse of dissidents. In fact, this is completely inaccurate. It is true that some communists have been occasionally arrested recently, but they are related to a long-solved conspiracy case that is being tried for endangering national security, and not people who voted against Hitler in this election. Foreign newspapers are spreading rumors wantonly in order to sensationalize, which is absolutely untrue." (Havas, 23rd)

(Munich) As a result of President Hitler's amnesty, 402 political prisoners and 1,610 criminal prisoners were released from Bavarian prisons today. Several thousand other suspects have been exempted from prosecution. (Reuters, 23rd)

Hitler assassination untrue

(Munich) Foreign rumors say Premier Hitler was assassinated. An Associated Press reporter here inquired with Hitler himself by telephone late at night, and the reply was that the assassination story was completely untrue. (Guomin News, 23rd)

German-Polish Trade Agreement Negotiations

Allowing the exchange of military supplies in wartime

Will affect the Franco-Polish alliance

(Paris) The Paris Echo reports that Berlin and Warsaw have been negotiating a trade agreement for quite some time, and significant progress has been made in recent weeks. The two countries will conclude an agreement on a completely reciprocal basis, stipulating that Poland should supply Germany with food and raw materials, and Germany should export an equal amount of manufactured goods and chemicals to Poland. This agreement also includes secret clauses stipulating that in the event of war, Poland should supply Germany with food and raw materials. The Paris Echo concludes, "From this agreement, it can be foreseen that if Germany goes to war with someone, Poland will declare its independence. With such an agreement, the alliance between France and Poland will naturally be abolished, and Poland's obligations under the League of Nations Covenant will also be denied." (Havas, 24th)

Japan Develops European and American Shipping Routes

(London) It is heard that Nippon Yusen Kaisha, based on Japan's new shipping subsidies, plans to add several fast passenger and cargo ships to the shipping routes between Europe and Asia. Because most of the company's ships on these routes are old and slow. The company also recognizes that the number of passengers and cargo between San Francisco and Japan is increasing, so it also intends to increase the number of ships on this route. It is heard that the United States is determined not to discuss subsidies at the International Shipping Chamber of Commerce meeting to be held in London in October. The United States is willing to consider the problem of surplus ships, but people in the shipping industry believe that this meeting may not have much effect. (Reuters, 24th)

Cai Tingkai Arrives in New York

Welcome plane crashes

(New York) Cai Tingkai, former commander of the Chinese 19th Route Army, arrived here on a tour of the United States. Two Chinese aviators flew to Cortis Airport today to welcome him by the sea and perform aerial displays. Unexpectedly, the two planes collided in the air, resulting in an accident. At that time, Mr. Cai had not yet arrived in port. The two aviators, one Mr. Weng and one Mr. Kang, took off and performed aerial acrobatics before heading to the sea. One of them suddenly lost control, and the two planes collided in the air. Mr. Weng's plane fell on the roof of an apartment building, and Mr. Weng was killed instantly. Mr. Kang was able to force a landing at the airport with minor injuries. Later, after an investigation by the U.S. Department of Commerce, it was learned that Mr. Weng's plane had had an accident in 1932. The Department of Commerce refused to issue a pilot's license because it was unsuitable for flying. (Guomin News, 23rd)

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's New Ship

The "Haiheng" holds a launching ceremony in England

Named by Mrs. Guo, the ambassador

(London) The "Haiheng" steamer, ordered by China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in England, was launched in Glasgow today. During the ceremony, Chinese Ambassador Guo opened the Chinese national flag, and everyone bowed three times to it. After Mrs. Guo named the ship, the new ship slid into the sea amidst the sound of firecrackers. This ship has special equipment to prevent pirates. Key points are separated by iron railings, and passengers of different classes are also separated. Ambassador Guo said in his speech that the launching of the "Haiheng" is an important undertaking from the Chinese perspective and can be regarded as a revival of China's coastal shipping industry, just as the launching of Britain's No. 534 large merchant ship can be regarded as a revival of Britain's maritime shipping industry. (Reuters, 23rd)

Andong's flood is disastrous

(Beiping) Foreigners received a telegram from Andong: more than a thousand houses in Andong city have been washed away by the water, and about 8,000 houses are in danger of collapsing. According to the river's normal water level of 7.5 feet, it has risen a total of 5.5 feet. If the weather clears up in the short term, there may not be any danger. (Special Dispatch, 24th)

An expert talks about the silver issue

(Nanjing) London believes that if China does not block silver exports, it can satisfy the United States' desire to purchase silver, and China can also increase gold imports and gradually implement the gold standard. According to an expert, China is a silver standard country, and the more silver in the country, the better. Current silver exports are harmful. If there is too little silver in the country, the turnover will be sluggish, which can easily lead to economic panic and social unrest. After the nationalization of silver, China, which uses the most silver, is even more cautious. The United States purchases silver from abroad, and Britain also purchases it secretly. If China cannot ban silver exports, a large amount will flow out. London's purchase seems to have two effects: first, if all the silver is concentrated in the United States, the European economic community will inevitably be constrained by it. Therefore, Britain is also secretly trying to buy silver from all parties to show its resistance to the United States. Second, China is the country with the most silver reserves in the world. Britain, witnessing the large amount of silver in China being bought by the United States, is very jealous and deliberately makes this publicity so that China's silver will not be completely bought by the United States, and Britain can also buy a part to prevent future troubles. (Special Dispatch, 24th)

International Commercial Telegraph

│Special commercial report by Reuters on August 24th│

(Gold and Silver) London Gold Price: The London gold price today was 139 shillings and 3 pence, up 7.5 pence.

London Silver: The London silver market remained stable today. The United States, India, and speculators bought in, and China sold out. The spot and futures prices were both 21 pence and 0.5625, the same as yesterday.

(Exchange Rates) Anglo-American: Continental Europe sold off pounds sterling in today's London foreign exchange market, fearing further devaluation of the US dollar. The Anglo-American exchange rate opened at $5.08375, down 0.25 from yesterday's US-British closing exchange rate. The price continued to fall before noon, down a total of 1.3125, so the exchange rate at 2:00 PM was $5.070625.

(Franco-British) Opened at 75 francs 93, up 3 pounds sterling, but fell 15 pounds sterling at 11:00, to 75 francs 78. This price remained unchanged until 2:00 PM.

(US-British) The New York foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The pound sterling followed the trend of the London exchange market, opening weakly, down 1.625, so the US-British opening price was $5.07. This price remained unchanged before noon.

(Cotton and Wheat) US Cotton: The cotton market was stable. The price before noon was slightly lower than yesterday's closing price. Purchases by Liverpool and other firms absorbed small-scale hedging and profit-taking. (British Cotton) The Liverpool cotton market also rose slightly today. The October futures price at 1:00 PM was 6.88, up 2 pounds sterling.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market price rose today. The October futures price at 1:00 PM was 5 shillings and 10.75 pence, up 0.375.

US Wheat: The wheat market opening price was 103.5, up 0.25, because the Liverpool wheat market was better.

(Rubber) London: The London rubber market was quiet today. The transaction price for October-December was 7.625 pence, down 0.0625 from yesterday's close. New York: The rubber opened, down 15 points, but later showed some improvement.

(Securities) New York: Before the opening of the New York securities market, the factors that were beneficial to the market were (1) the trading volume decreased with the market price reaction, and (2) the price of securities exchange broker seats did not indicate a decline in popularity. Buyers could meet with prices not far from the last purchase price, but the highest price currently is $160,000. The last sale price was $95,000. The factors that were unfavorable to the market were (1) a general lack of trust in the future of the business, and (2) there is currently no certainty about the wheat tax on foreign operators. When the securities market opened this morning, the price fluctuations were quite stable. Although there were ups and downs, most were limited to zero. People in the market seemed to want to proceed cautiously and wait for a turnaround in the business and a clear sign of development in Washington. Hangzhou Reporters Association

Prepares to Celebrate Reporters' Day

(Hangzhou) The 5th Members' Congress of the Hangzhou Reporters Association once telegraphed reporters' associations across the country, stipulating September 1st as Reporters' Day. At that time, they stated their reasons and telegraphed for the agreement of reporters' associations in various places. Recently, in order to implement the resolution of the congress, they also appointed personnel to prepare for the celebration. Reporters' associations in Bian, Su, and Han sent telegrams to inquire about the reasons for the commemoration and expressed their willingness to assist in the process. The Hangzhou Reporters Association sent another telegram to the whole country on the 23rd, stating briefly that although the development of the news industry and the protection of journalists had been approved by the National Congress and handed over to the National Government for handling, it had also been virtually shelved. It was not until September 1, 1933, that the Executive Yuan approved a letter from the Central Executive Committee, specifically ordering the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Military Affairs to issue notices to the provincial and municipal governments and various military organs, stating that personnel engaged in the news industry should be effectively protected (see Nanjing telegram from September 1, last year). The Hangzhou Reporters Association took the government's explicit order to effectively protect the safety of reporters as the beginning, and in order to support the implementation of the central government's decrees, it specifically decided that September 1st would be Reporters' Day to commemorate this event, and requested unanimous support. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 24th)

Hangzhou City Water Supply High in Salt

Pujiang Displays Signs of Food and Water Shortages

(Hangzhou) Hangzhou's tap water is now high in salt. Wealthy people are buying Tiger Spring water at high prices. Temple monks are hoarding this rare commodity, making ten times the profit. Most citizens are buying and drinking only salt water every day. The people are panicked and unable to express their anxieties. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 24th)

(Hangzhou) The 220,000 people of Pujiang County in eastern Zhejiang are currently showing signs of food and water shortages. It is estimated that the county's harvest will be less than 10%. Bandits are also taking the opportunity to rise up. Small and medium-sized landlords and farmers in rural areas are headed for total ruin. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 23rd)
