Japanese Rice Chemical Test Shows It Contains Toxic Bacteria

Difficult to Digest, Forbidden for Consumption Even in Japan

Changqi Correspondence: Japan is also experiencing a severe drought this year, and rice prices are soaring. It is reported that some Japanese rice is being sold in Shanghai disguised as domestic rice. According to reports, this rice is more than 20 or 30 years old and was hoarded for military use. Because of the abundant harvests in Japan in the past two years, this old rice was sold abroad to make room for newly harvested rice. Last year, Japanese doctors chemically tested this old rice and found that it seemed to contain a kind of toxic bacteria, which caused a feeling of fullness and difficulty in digestion after consumption. The Japanese authorities had forbidden the public from eating it. Also, in February of this year, the Japanese side wanted to dump this rice on a certain country, and it was all transported to one place for storage, piling up like a mountain. Later, after the country telegraphed to refuse import, the rice was piled up in front of our consulate and customs on empty ground, reaching more than 30,000 bags. After half a month, it was moved away. (New Sound News Agency)

Huang River Breach at Changyuan

Reaches Shou Zhang County in Shandong Province

Passes Through Pu County and Fan County in Two Days

The Speed of the Water is Very Rapid

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River breach at Changyuan entered Shandong Province on the 21st, and passed Daokou in the territory of Pu County to Fan County on the 22nd. When the water was in Hebei Province, it was five or six inches high and thirty or forty zhang wide, and its progress was slow. After entering Shandong, the water was more than one foot high, only seven-tenths of a zhang wide, and the flow rate was five li per hour, and it could travel 120 li in one day and night. It traveled eastward along the Jin River dike, following the old path of the breach last year. Presumably, after passing through Shou Zhang, it will still enter the main river from Taochengbu in Dong'e. Fortunately, the crops along the way were not greatly damaged. Zhang Lianjia, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, set off on the 21st to inspect the upper reaches of the Yellow River and spent the night at Luokou. He sailed upstream on the 22nd to inspect Taochengbu. Xu Desheng, the section chief of the north bank, telegraphed the River Affairs Bureau about the situation of the floodwaters reaching Fan County. In addition to reporting to the Provincial Government's Department of Civil Affairs, the bureau also telegraphed the county magistrates of Fan County, Shou Zhang, Yanggu, and Dong'e, and the first and second sections of the north bank to be on full alert. The upstream Shaan County suddenly rose by 1.59 meters on the 21st, and the water level dropped to 293.33 meters early on the 22nd. In the afternoon, it dropped again to 292.48 meters, and the situation turned and eased. The water rose in the province in the morning and was slightly stable in the afternoon.

In addition, the Yellow River breach at Changyuan entered Shandong Province on the 21st, and passed Pu County to Fan County on the 22nd. At noon, it passed Fan County and flowed eastward, flowing very quickly. Today (the 23rd), the River Affairs Bureau received reports from Chengfang Committee member Ren Shaoquan and section chief Xu Desheng that the water had reached Jinjiying in Shou Zhang at Chen hour [7-9am], with a water depth of one foot and a width of more than 20 zhang. Daokou in Fan County was flooded. Also, according to a report from Yang Jifeng, the county magistrate of Yanggu County, the water reached the Jiangjia Alley in Yanggu. The Jin River dike on the north bank was firmly built, and the waves on the south bank needed to be leveled. If the water is not too high, the area north of the Jin River may be safe. In the afternoon, the River Affairs Bureau received another report from the upper reaches that the flood had reached Miaotai at the junction of Shou Zhang and Yanggu, which is 18 li upstream of Shou Zhang. Today, the water level of the entire river has increased. Zhang Lianjia, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, inspected the upper reaches and traveled upstream from Fan County this morning to inspect Gaodukou at the junction of Hebei and Shandong. In the afternoon, he returned to Fan County. (The 23rd)

Hebei Provincial Government

Relief for the Victims of Changyuan

Appropriates 5,000 Yuan to First Provide Emergency Relief

Sends Lin Chengxiu to the Disaster Area for Inspection

Tianjin Correspondence: Changyuan in southern Hebei has recently suffered a severe flood due to the Yellow River breach. The city of Changyuan is surrounded by four or five feet of water. Fortunately, the breach in the Yellow River levee has slowed down somewhat in the past week, and the Post-Disaster Reconstruction Office is making every effort to close it. As of the 19th, the water level on the outskirts of Changyuan had dropped by five inches. However, because Puyang is low-lying, the floodwaters from various breaches are gradually spreading in that direction. On the 20th, the county magistrate of that county telegraphed that the floodwaters were only 20 li from the city and would likely inundate the county within a day or two. The county immediately gathered laborers to build small embankments to prevent the water from rising. Yesterday, the Hebei Provincial Government received telegrams from Hu Yuanhui, Director of the Yellow River Post-Disaster Reconstruction Office, and his deputy, Sun Qingze, stating that the floodwaters at the breach were stable and that the breaches at Zhangxinzhai and Xiangli, which had been washed away, had been strengthened with willow fences. Workers were being supervised to build willow fences at the Jiugulu Jiaozhai breach. If the water level does not rise within three days, it should be possible to close the breach. The Provincial Government, in addition to telegraphed to the central government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of Finance, reporting the dangerous situation, and requested funds to relieve the victims of the flood in Changyuan, and because Changyuan was the first to bear the brunt of the disaster, tens of thousands of victims were living in the open, crying from hunger and cold, waiting for relief, it ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to send Commissioner Wang Zhilin, together with Yang Shulin, the relief commissioner of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Committee, to the disaster area for investigation, and ordered him to temporarily withdraw 5,000 yuan from the Changyuan branch of the Hebei Provincial Bank to provide emergency relief. The official arrived in the disaster area on the 20th to assist Changyuan County Magistrate Bu Hengxu in providing emergency relief. Representatives of the Changyuan, Puyang, and Dongguang Yellow River Disaster Relief Associations in Tianjin said that the funds allocated by the province for relief were a drop in the bucket and would not solve the problem, and on the 19th they telegraphed various departments and ministries of the central government, calling for immediate relief. Charitable organizations here will also send personnel to the disaster area for inspection within a few days, and then discuss ways to provide relief. Lin Chengxiu, Director of the Hebei Construction Department, went to Tianjin by car on the evening of the 18th to inspect the situation at the breach and then transferred to the Pinghan Road to go there. According to the Hebei authorities, there is no other way to temporarily block the breach, except to add willow fences to temporarily block it. Engineering work such as building dams with sand and stone can only be carried out after the water recedes. According to the report of the Post-Disaster Reconstruction Office, this year's Yellow River breach was mostly at the site of the breach last year. Although the Post-Disaster Reconstruction Office closed it this spring, the sandy soil was loose and the reinforcement was not strong, so it collapsed after being impacted by a large flow of water. Although this is not entirely the truth, the construction funds for the Yellow River Post-Disaster Levee really require more than 2.9 million yuan according to the project estimate, and even if the cost is reduced as much as possible, it will still require more than 2.4 million yuan. The Hebei province has sent the Director of the Construction Department to Beijing several times to face the Finance Department and state the requirements for raising funds, and requested that they find a way to allocate funds. The Ministry also intends to extend the addition of Changlu salt tax for another two years and to borrow from the banking sector. After the Hebei authorities negotiated with the banking sector, the banking sector refused because the salt tax surcharge had been used as collateral for several loans, and if it was extended for another two years, the term of the current loan would be too long and the guarantee was doubtful. In order to rush the construction, the Provincial Bank advanced 700,000 yuan three times to barely repair the embankments. There was less money and more work, and it was not easy to make it strong. Therefore, when the province appointed the Director of the Post-Disaster Reconstruction Office, they all declined because the responsibility was heavy and it was not easy to succeed. Finally, Hu Yuanhui, a member of the Provincial Committee, was appointed concurrently, and Sun Qingze, Director of the Yellow River River Affairs Bureau, was appointed as deputy. Now, it is indeed because of the lack of funds and simple work that the accident has happened. (The 21st)

Three Provinces Bandit Suppression Headquarters

Executes Illegal Military Officers by Firing Squad

For Embezzling Public Funds and Deducting Military Pay

Obvious Evidence of Corruption, Tyranny, and Atrocious Acts

Hankou Correspondence: Shi Kun, the captain of the First Transport Brigade of the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Three Provinces Bandit Suppression Headquarters, had been in office for two months and had embezzled public funds, deducted supplies, abused soldiers, bullied merchants, and engaged in prostitution and procuring prostitutes. Zhang Xueliang, the deputy commander, found out about this, sent personnel to investigate, and found it to be true. He was executed by firing squad on the 23rd, and a notice was sent to the military and political organs of the three provinces, announcing the crimes. The original order is as follows: The case of Shi Kun, the former captain of the First Transport Brigade of this headquarters, who was corrupt, tyrannical, lawless, and undisciplined, has been investigated by this headquarters. All the facts of the crime have been admitted without denial. In May, he deducted 108 yuan and 92 cents in supplies, embezzled 84 yuan and 77 cents from dismissed personnel, falsely reported 30 yuan and 40 cents in rice, and arbitrarily fined officials' salaries for his own benefit 14 yuan and 40 cents. In June, the amount withheld and not distributed, intending to embezzle, included 280 yuan in supplies and 32 yuan and 46 cents in falsely reported military shoes. In addition, he occupied more than 460 yuan of public funds. In total, Shi Kun, who had been in office for less than two months, deducted, falsely reported, embezzled, and occupied a total of more than 1,000 yuan. In addition, he privately set up a sales agency, operated his own business, used excuses to collect money, and sold tobacco, alcohol, grain, and fruit, forcing soldiers to buy from him, thereby greatly relaxing the prohibition on tobacco and alcohol. He also abused his power, abused soldiers, relied on his power and acted recklessly, bullied merchants, and engaged in prostitution and debauchery. Recently, he even induced a widow from the people to become his fourth wife, sent soldiers to take turns guarding her, and arbitrarily beat her, causing injury. His crimes are outrageous. At this time of bandit suppression, Shi Kun, as a military officer, should have been dedicated to his duty, abide by the law, and be honest and self-disciplined. How could he have committed so many crimes in less than two months of service? If he is not punished to the fullest extent of the law, how can we curb corruption and warn the tyrannical? In addition to executing Shi Kun by firing squad and issuing separate orders, we hereby order you to know and instruct your subordinates to know this order. (The 23rd)

Jiujiang Drought Relief Association Established

Severe Disaster, No Harvest

Submits a Request to the Government to Allocate Funds for Relief

Jiujiang Correspondence: This year's drought in our county is unprecedented in decades. Since transplanting rice seedlings, the drought demon has wreaked havoc. There has been no rain for two months, and the land is all red. The victims are on the roads, and the tragedy is extreme. The local officials and people from all walks of life held a county-wide disaster relief meeting at the Jiujiang County Party Headquarters on the 8th of this month. The congress decided to organize a special agency called the Jiujiang County Drought Relief Committee, and publicly elected 21 members, including ex officio members and standing committee members, to carry out disaster relief matters. It was officially established on that day, and Committee Member Luo Bocheng, Committee Member Xiong Bangyan, and Committee Member Xiao Mian were sent to Guling to personally meet with Chairman Chiang, Executive Yuan President Wang, Finance Minister Kong, and Provincial Government Chairman Xiong, to personally present the disaster situation and appeal for relief. At the same time, Committee Member Wu Zhenya was sent to the province to personally meet with Lu, Chairman of the Jiangxi Provincial Relief Association, Xiong, Chairman of the Provincial Government, and Wu, Director of the Department of Finance, to actively carry out the work. The presentation is copied below: "To present the extraordinarily severe disaster situation and earnestly request the allocation of emergency relief to save the people's lives. Jiujiang is mostly mountainous and is known as barren land. Droughts occur frequently, and the people's lives are difficult. This year's extraordinary disaster is unprecedented in decades. Since last winter, there has been little rain. After the spring, the ponds and weirs are dry. It is estimated that no more than 50-60% of the high and low fields in the county could be planted. Since the beginning of summer, there has been a severe drought for two months. The tens of thousands of acres have all turned red. Now that the autumn harvest is approaching, there is no harvest. Alas, what can our farmers rely on for their lives? Since the 16th year of the Republic, we have suffered from banditry, and the villages have been devastated to the extreme. Now the granaries are empty and there is no bran to eat. In ten families, several do not light fires. In one village, the smoke from cooking has been cut off for days. There are frequent incidents of families committing suicide. The sound of selling wives and pawning children is endless. At this time of impending death, if we do not appeal for relief, we fear that the 300,000 people in the county will either starve to death or go astray. Looking to the future, there is great hidden worry. Bocheng and others, seeing the urgency of the situation and being close to the capital, took the liberty to humbly beg you to consider the serious disaster situation in Xun, bestow special favor, allocate large amounts of money, distribute emergency relief, get them out of the water and fire and ascend to the mats, spread the grace over the wounds and wear the imperial heaven on the later earth, and be deeply grateful. If there is anything appropriate, it should be presented. We beg you to examine and implement it. Jiujiang County Drought Relief Committee, Director Luo Bocheng".

Xiamen Pirates Rob Ship

Longsheng Small Steamer Encountered Bandits Between Wutong and Aotou

Pirates Shot and Killed One Passenger, Losses of 3,000 Yuan

Xiamen Correspondence: The Longsheng small steamer of the Longde Shipping Company in this city, with a displacement of over 100 tons, departed from Tong'an for Xiamen at about 5 PM on the 16th, carrying 75 passengers and goods such as sugar cane, tea, taro, and longan. About 20 minutes after departure, the ship arrived near Wutongdu of Bingzhou, opposite Xiamen, between the northern inner harbor of Xiamen and Aotou. Suddenly, six passengers each took out handguns, occupied the pilothouse and engine room, and fired several shots. One bullet hit the compass in the pilothouse, and one hit the deck of the engine room. The helmsman Hong Sidu and his assistant Ye Ai were watched and forced to steer the ship eastward. The engine room was also watched by two pirates at the same time. The remaining two pirates searched the passengers by name. One of the passengers, Chen Wanlai, recognized the pirate. Because Chen lived in Shanhouting Township in Tong'an and was disturbed by bandits, he planned to file a complaint with the county government. The bandit leader Chen Tianshang found out about this and had Wanlai tied up and held for ransom. Later, the garrison troops, according to a report from Wanlai's family, sent troops to encircle and suppress the bandits, and rescued him. Since then, the bandits had been spying on him, repeatedly trying to get Chen to satisfy their vengeance. Chen then boarded the Longsheng steamer to escape to Xiamen. Unexpectedly, the pirates who robbed the ship were the same gang who had tied up Chen. Knowing that he could not escape, Chen said to a passenger next to him, "The pirates know me. I cannot avoid death. Please take this yuan as a fare. After you escape, go to Hong Benbu Yuanyuan in Xiamen and report to Hong Hongru, the chairman of the Xiamen General Chamber of Commerce, and ask him to avenge me. Chairman Hong is my maternal uncle." After Chen finished speaking, he curled up at the stern of the cabin. He was then searched out, and the bandit cursed loudly and shot him twice, once in the chest and once in the shoulder. He then kicked Chen's body into the sea. At 6:30 PM, the ship arrived at Yu Island. Because the helmsman was steering according to the pirate's directions and was not familiar with the route, it ran aground on the sand. There was already a sailboat there, and as the ship drew alongside, seven pirates also boarded the ship and fired randomly, injuring two passengers. They also searched them and moved the silver objects onto the boat, abandoning the longan and tea. They set sail towards Qiongtou, across the sea from Xiamen. At that time, it was 7 PM, and the sky was already dark. A little later, two other boats approached the Longsheng and chased after the pirate ship. When they arrived at Qiongtou, the pirates went ashore. The larger of the two boats went towards Tong'an, and the smaller one slowly towed the pirate ship. Just then, Lin Zhencheng, the head of the Xiamen Heshan Office, heard that the ship had been robbed and led detectives to chase after them on the Heqiao gunboat, using searchlights to shine around. Seeing the ship, he shouted for it to stop. The people in the boat did not respond, so he opened fire. The helmsman Yang Yin was shot and killed. The gunboat then took the sailboat and the pirate ship back. There were three people in the sailboat and two boatmen who had been tied up in the pirate ship. According to them, they were all forced by the pirates to use their boats and were forced to drive them. The Longsheng steamer waited for the tide to rise and arrived in Xiamen at 9 PM. All the passengers escaped. The Heqiao gunboat patrolled the sea between Wutong and Aotou and returned at dawn. The five people captured from the sailboat and the pirate ship included (1) Xie Shuiping, from Jinmen; (2) Lin Shui, from Tong'an; (3) Wang Chao; (4) Wang Zhang; (5) Cai Yong. According to them, they were all boatmen who were forced by the pirates to use their boats and were forced to drive them. The corpse was examined by the court. According to the passengers, the two sailboats that arrived later seemed to be reinforcements from the pirates. The larger one went to Tong'an, and the smaller one took the sailboat away, which seemed to have been left behind by the pirates. According to the Heshan Office's investigation, Yang Yin, who was shot and killed, was indeed a pirate who robbed the ship. Also, Xie Shuiping, Lin Shui, and Cai Yong, three of the five people arrested, were identified as pirates by the passengers. No one identified Wang Chao and Wang Zhang, who were indeed tied up at the time. The total loss on the ship was all the silver objects carried by the passengers, totaling approximately 3,800 yuan. (The 20th)

Merchant

Debtor Liquidation Ordinance Full Text (Continued)

Article 39: The debtor shall explain the proposed settlement plan at the creditors' meeting. If the debtor proposes the settlement plan only at the creditors' meeting and has a person who bears any collateral or joint responsibility, that person shall be invited to attend the meeting. The terms of the proposed settlement plan may be changed at the creditors' meeting. Article 40: The debtor shall attend the creditors' meeting in person unless there is a legitimate reason and the court permits the appointment of an agent. The aforementioned agent shall submit documents proving his authority. Article 41: The creditors' meeting may make resolutions on the following matters: (1) Granting necessary living expenses to the debtor and their family; (2) Suspension or continuation of the debtor's business; (3) Methods for safekeeping valuable items; (4) Appointing a supervisor to oversee and assist the liquidator; (5) Replacing the liquidator or restricting their authority; (6) Matters submitted by the court for discussion. The aforementioned resolution requires the consent of more than half of the creditors present, and whose claims exceed half of the total claims of those present. Article 42: The creditors' meeting shall resolve on the settlement plan. The settlement plan's approval requires the consent of more than half of the creditors present, and whose claims reach more than three-quarters of the total declared claims. If the settlement plan is not approved, and one of the two conditions stipulated in the preceding paragraph is met, the court shall schedule a continued meeting. The same applies if creditors who meet the conditions in paragraph 2 of the preceding article agree to continue the meeting. Article 43: The number of creditors, the amount of their claims, and the total amount of claims as calculated in paragraph 2 of Article 41 and paragraph 2 of the preceding article, shall be limited to those creditors who have the right to vote. Creditors who have joined the liquidation, the liquidator, and the debtor who have no objection to the declared claims, their creditors have the right to vote based on the amount of the declared claims. If there is any objection, the creditor may exercise the right to object and the court shall decide on the amount to be exercised. Article 44: A creditor may appoint an agent to attend the meeting and exercise voting rights. The aforementioned agent shall submit documents proving his authority. Article 45: If the creditors' meeting is to be postponed or continued, it need not be announced or summon the parties concerned if the court announces it on the spot. Article 46: Resolutions made by the creditors' meeting in accordance with the provisions of Article 41 may be executed only after being approved by the court. Article 47: If the settlement plan is approved by the creditors' meeting, the court shall immediately on that date, or on a designated date, make a ruling on whether to approve the settlement. The aforementioned designated date shall be announced on the spot and need not be announced or summon the parties concerned. Creditors, liquidators, and debtors who have joined the liquidation may state their opinions on whether or not the settlement should be approved. Article 48: A ruling not approving the settlement shall not be made unless one of the following circumstances exists: (1) The procedure or resolution regarding the settlement violates the provisions of the law, and the deficiency cannot be corrected; (2) The debtor has engaged in fraudulent behavior against creditors; (3) The settlement resolution was formed by improper means; (4) The settlement resolution is contrary to the general interests of creditors. Article 49: The ruling to approve or disapprove the settlement shall be announced and its gist shall be publicized. An appeal may be filed against the aforementioned ruling. Article 50: The settlement takes effect when the ruling approving it becomes final. Article 51: After the ruling approving the settlement becomes final, the court clerk shall record the terms of the settlement in the creditor list. Article 52: After the ruling approving the settlement becomes final, the debtor shall immediately pay off the claims arising from legal principles and the liquidation procedure expenses. Article 53: After the settlement, the debtor shall comply with the restrictions stipulated in the settlement terms regarding the management and disposal of their property. Article 54: The settlement shall be effective for the benefit and detriment of creditors who are entitled to join the liquidation under Article 31, regardless of whether they have joined. Article 55: If the debtor fails to perform in accordance with the settlement, the creditors whose claims have not been fulfilled may revoke the concessions stipulated in the settlement. The revocation of concessions shall not affect the rights obtained by the creditor due to the settlement. The creditor may not exercise the right to the amount of the claim recovered due to the revocation of concessions until the settlement has been fully performed. Article 56: If the debtor fails to perform in accordance with the settlement, and if more than half of the creditors who have declared their claims, and whose claims reach more than three-quarters of the total declared claims, petition, the court shall revoke the settlement by ruling. Creditors who have received full performance in accordance with the settlement shall not be counted in the number of people required for the aforementioned petition. Those who have received full or partial performance shall have the amount they have received deducted from the original claim amount, and the remaining amount shall be counted in the amount of claims required for the aforementioned petition. The revocation of the settlement shall not affect the rights obtained by the creditor due to the settlement. Article 57: If the court revokes the settlement, it shall announce the gist of its ruling. The same applies to rejecting the petition for revocation. An appeal may be filed against the aforementioned ruling. Article 58: In one of the following circumstances, the court shall declare the debtor bankrupt upon petition or ex officio: 1. The debtor fails to propose a settlement plan before the end of the creditors' meeting; 2. The settlement plan proposed by the debtor is withdrawn before it is approved by the creditors; 3. The settlement plan has not been approved within two months from the date of the first creditors' meeting; 4. The ruling disapproving the settlement becomes final; 5. The ruling revoking the settlement becomes final. After declaring bankruptcy in accordance with the provisions of the preceding paragraph, the previous liquidation procedure shall be regarded as a bankruptcy procedure and continued. Article 59: The provisions of this Ordinance regarding settlement shall apply mutatis mutandis to debtors who propose a settlement plan in bankruptcy proceedings. Article 60: Liquidation cases shall be handled by a single judge. Appeal cases in the liquidation procedure shall be decided by the collegiate panel of the local court before the implementation of the three-instance system. Article 61: Rulings made in the liquidation procedure may not be appealed, except as otherwise specifically provided for in this Ordinance. Appeals may be filed by anyone who has an interest in the original ruling. If the ruling has been announced, the appeal period shall be calculated uniformly from the date the announcement takes effect. Article 62: The ruling of the appellate court shall take effect only after it becomes final, but the court may stipulate in the ruling that it shall take effect immediately. If the appellate court declares liquidation, it shall take effect immediately. Article 63: Rulings made in the liquidation procedure may be revoked or changed by the court that made the ruling, except for those regarding the commencement or termination of liquidation. Article 64: When making announcements in accordance with the provisions of this Ordinance, the announcement documents shall be posted at the court's notice board and published in newspapers. If there are no newspapers that can be published within the jurisdiction of the court, they shall also be posted at the chamber of commerce or other equivalent places. In addition to the provisions of the preceding paragraph, the court may also order the announcement documents to be published in the gazette. Announcements published in newspapers shall take effect on the day following the last publication date, and those not published in newspapers shall take effect three days after posting. Article 65: In accordance with the provisions of this Ordinance, when service is made in addition to the announcement, the service may be done by delivering the documents to the post office. Article 66: The court shall prepare the original text or copies of the following documents for interested parties to read at any time: 1. Documents regarding the application for declaration of legal principles and the settlement plan; 2. The investigation record or report of Article 6, the sealing or marking record of Article 19, and the property list and balance sheet of Article 20; 3. Documents regarding the declared claims and the creditor list. Article 67: Unless otherwise specifically provided for in this Ordinance regarding the liquidation procedure, Article 68 of the Code of Civil Procedure shall apply mutatis mutandis. Article 68: This Ordinance shall come into effect from the date of its promulgation. (23rd)

Songjiang

Fellow Townsmen in Shanghai

Please Investigate the Case of Corruption in Land Tax

To President Wang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, President Yu of the Supervisory Yuan, Chairman Jiang of the Nanchang Branch, and Chairman Chen of the Zhenjiang Provincial Government: In the case of the Songjiang converted land tax, the county magistrate Jin Tigan included the northern part of the Pu area into the southern part of the Pu area when applying for tax reduction, which is already a breach of duty. After the application for tax reduction was approved last year, he did not cancel the printed strings, issue announcements, or return the floating mortgages. Instead, he deducted more than 10,000 piculs of tax rice from the actual collection amount and the uncollected amount of the autumn survey each year, which is obviously intentional behavior. He colluded with the chief of the finance section, Che Zhao, and the director of the eastern counter collection, Ye Zongcheng, to embezzle more than 3,000 piculs of converted land tax from the northern part of the Pu area and 2,000 piculs from the southern part of the Pu area (originally 7,000 piculs, calculated based on 2,000 piculs collected) from the 18th to 21st years of the Republic, totaling more than 100,000 yuan. He also concealed 60% of the tax silver in the northern part of the Pu area and the hinterland of the southern part of the Pu area in the 22nd year (only 40% was remitted out of 100% actually collected), totaling more than 10,000 yuan. The facts are clear and the evidence is solid. He used the benevolent policies of the provincial government and the blood and sweat of farmers as a hunting ground for corruption and embezzlement. If this is not punished, where is the national law? The case involves embezzlement of public funds, and we dare not remain silent. We specially telegraph to request your Excellencies to punish according to law, so as to warn corrupt officials and emphasize national taxes. Fellow Townsmen in Shanghai, Zhang Shutong, Ma Yinliang, Wang Yaoqin, Wang Qingsheng, Qiu Hongzhang, Zhang Zunan, Qian Dingda, Lu Hongsheng, Zhang Yiping, Li Menggeng.

Suzhou

Two Major Lake Tai Bandits Executed by Firing Squad

The provincial security team stationed in the southern warehouse of Wujiang captured two major Lake Tai bandits, Li Haishan and Wang Baoming, in March. They were sent to the province for interrogation. The bandits confessed that they had committed many crimes in Wujiang County, including the robbery of the Sujia liner, etc. They were sent back to Wujiang County for trial. After interrogation, it was confirmed that they were guilty and sentenced to death. The Jiangsu Provincial Government approved the sentence. On the 23rd, Xu, the county magistrate of Wujiang County, verified the identity of the two criminals, tied them to the execution ground outside the East Gate, and executed them by firing squad.

Verdict on Murder Case Outside Qimen

Li Shenggen, a villager from Tangjiazhuang Township outside Qimen in Suzhou, colluded with Lu Rensheng, who runs a butcher shop, to beat his niece-in-law, Lu Meimei, to death. The District Procuratorate detained Li Shenggen and Lu Rensheng for interrogation, and verified that Li Meimei did die from her injuries. The trial has been concluded, and the verdict was announced yesterday: Lu Rensheng was sentenced to ten years of imprisonment, and Li Shenggen was acquitted.

Haimen

Dispute Over Competition Among Chauffeurs

Since the completion of the Ling-Lyu Road (Lingdian Port to Lvsi) in the Fourth District's Lingdian Port, there has been a large number of passengers traveling back and forth. Chauffeurs Lu Chulang, Yuan Jinbo, Hong Youzhang, etc., organized a joint ticket office, hoping to monopolize the business. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday (21st), a Lu Longsheng car, carrying five passengers, was about to leave for Lvsi when Lu Chulang and others saw it, stopped it from driving, and ordered it to buy tickets. Lu Longsheng refused, and a conflict broke out. Lu Chulang, Yuan Jinbo, Hong Youzhang, etc., used benches to smash Lu Longsheng's car and severely injured his waist, causing him to faint on the spot. His family managed to rescue him, but his life is in critical condition. Yesterday (22nd), he filed a complaint with the county government. After Xu, the judge, verified the facts, he ordered the arrest of the perpetrators for interrogation.

Public Security Third Bureau

Patrol Chief and Squad Leader Detained

Lu Kaishan, Chen Gongyu, and Chen Yuezong, the patrol chief and squad leader of the Public Security Third Bureau in Sanyang Town, neglected their duties and privately collected illegal fees. The director, Huang Mingxiang, was unaware of this. The day before yesterday, Gong Huaizhi and others from the local area filed a complaint with the superiors. Lu Kaishan, Lin Xuehai, and Chen Gongyu were detained. Yesterday, they were sent to the County Public Security Bureau. The director, Hao Zhiying, was greatly angered and immediately shackled the three criminals and detained them, intending to send them to the county for handling.

Wuxi

Organizing the Electrical User Advancement Association

The Qishuyan Power Plant had a dispute with users over the issue of electricity deposit. Although the Chamber of Commerce discussed it once, no concrete solution has been reached. Yesterday, the users, represented by the initiators, held a discussion meeting for electricity users at the Tonggeng Hall in the park. Sun Xixia was elected as the temporary chairman, and the following key issues were resolved: (1) Organize the Wuxi Electrical User Advancement Association; (2) Elect Sun Xixia, Yang Yintan, Xu Weichen, Xue Mingjian, Li Tiping, Shi Qinglin, Xue Yijun and other thirty-one people as preparatory members; (3) Set the first preparatory meeting to be held at 4 pm on the 24th.

Construction Bureau Laying Telephone Lines in Meicun

The provincial long-distance telephone exchange office at the Tonghui Bridge has a rural telephone attached, and there are more than a dozen places in the four villages that have telephones connected to the switchboard. Recently, Meicun Town in the New Second District felt that there were many residents and that news was slow in the event of important events. It was urgent to add rural telephones. Therefore, a request was submitted to the county government and forwarded to the Construction Bureau. Construction work has begun immediately, and the cost is shared by the rural area and the government. The Construction Bureau has now approved it and sent personnel to Wuxi to work with the Construction Bureau and the exchange's engineering staff to start construction.

Chamber of Commerce Association Requests Reduction of Grain Business Tax

The joint meeting of directors and supervisors of the Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Association was held in the Gongyi Hall and Qiangzhai in Wujiang County this session. Fifty committee members attended, chaired by Yu Xiaochuan. The following key issues were resolved: (1) Grain is related to the people's livelihood. Currently, the drought is extremely severe, grain prices are soaring, and the business tax is being collected urgently. The association will continue to petition the provincial government to find ways to reduce it in order to maintain the people's livelihood; (2) Various exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies in various counties have been abolished by explicit orders, but the egg tax in Suqian County and the education rice tax collected on behalf of Wujiang County are onerous and burdensome. The association will immediately petition the provincial government to abolish them together; (3) It is reported that Jiangsu Province is issuing 30 million public bonds, and merchants will bear the brunt. At this time of popular poverty and financial exhaustion, and market decline, it is difficult for the people of Jiangsu to bear the burden. A telegram should be sent to the national government and various ministries to stop it immediately, and a telegram should be sent to the newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai to disclose the article for discussion in its original form, in order to arouse the attention of the people of Jiangsu; (4) Since the implementation of the new tariff, the import tax on cotton yarn and cotton fabrics has been reduced a lot, while the tax on hardware and machinery has increased, which has a great impact on the promotion of domestic goods and industrial and commercial enterprises. A petition should be submitted to the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry for review; (5) It is reported that a large amount of cash is being exported recently. National cash is like the blood of the human body. The outflow of blood will inevitably lead to depletion and death. Not only will the currency reserves be panicked, but all industries will perish with it. A telegram should be sent to the Economic Commission of the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry to find ways to stop it quickly.

Changzhou

Hall Committee Comes to Changzhou to Solicit Products

The Jiangsu Provincial Government has scheduled the Southeast Transportation Exhibition to be held in Hangzhou on October 10. Before the exhibition, it plans to hold a Jiangsu Provincial Goods Exhibition in the provincial capital in conjunction with the Provincial Party Department, and set up a market collection department in the exhibition, which will open on September 10. The best of the goods will be transferred to the Transportation Exhibition for display, and the goods from various counties are limited to be sent to the exhibition before September 5. Now the Construction Bureau believes that the deadline is approaching, and the goods sent by various counties are few. It specially sent a member, Chen Qiyuan, to Changzhou, who contacted the county government and the Chamber of Commerce on the 23rd, and discussed the plan with Shi Ziquan and Lin Jun, the directors of product collection in Wujin. It was decided to convene a meeting of various product agencies at Dengri to collect products at any time and send them to the exhibition for display on schedule. Chen also took a car to Wuxi that night.

Changshu

Police and Bandits Exchange Fire at Baimao Estuary

At about 9 pm on the 23rd, a person suddenly came to report to the Baimao Water Police Team that a large bandit ship was now berthed at the Baimao estuary. The ship was fully equipped with guns and carried sixty or seventy bandits, intending to rob the entire town of Baimao. It was also claimed that the person was a kidnapped hostage who had escaped from the ship. After receiving the report, the team first sent scouts to investigate, and the above situation was indeed found. Fearing that the police force was weak, it immediately telegraphed the Yuxun warship stationed in Huzhen and the urban defense team, and sent a squadron overnight to help suppress the bandits. When they arrived at the destination, they were unexpectedly detected by the bandit ship, which fired a gun to show its power. The police also opened fire in response. The gunfire lasted for about half an hour. Then the bandit ship sailed away across the river.

Nantong

Dispatching a Team to Search and Suppress Bandits in the Eastern Countryside

The Nantong District Security Command believed that bandits were lurking in the Yudongyi and Yuyu areas of the eastern countryside of Tongyi. They were carrying out large-scale activities, robbing and killing people, creating a situation of extreme terror. The security team has been dispatched to search and suppress the bandits in order to clear the source of the bandits.

Vice President of the Bar Association

Accused of Having an Affair with a Niece

The lawyer Wu Guixin is the vice president of the Nantong Bar Association. His wife, Li, has a niece named Xiangzhi, who is very beautiful. This year she is nineteen years old. Wu coveted her beauty and frequently showed enthusiasm, which eventually led to an affair. When the girl's father found out, he drove her away and published a notice in the newspaper to sever their father-daughter relationship. Later, the girl gave birth to a son, named Yongnian. Recently, she asked to marry Wu Guixin, but she was not tolerated by her aunt, Wu Li. Suddenly, Yongnian died of illness in Wu's house. Li Xiangzhi then accused Wu Guixin of seduction and breach of trust. The Procuratorate scheduled an investigation on the 25th. Unexpectedly, on the 22nd, Li Xiangzhi was chased, dragged, and tied onto a car by her aunt and Wu Guixin's secretary, Shi Zhiqi, etc., and driven away quickly on Nanda Street. The whereabouts of Li are currently unknown.

Jiaxing

Farmers Bank Has Resumed Business

After the Jiaxing County Farmers Bank had a major theft case, the manager, Wu Heshu, fled in fear of punishment. Xu Fukang and Tu Yiran, the staff members, were detained by the court for interrogation and sent to prison. Qian Mingzhu was released on bail by the Xiulun Silk Factory with a written guarantee of 3,000 yuan. Tu Danian was interrogated and found to be unrelated, and ordered to be released. Now the acting manager, Chen Zhigong, has started to reorganize the bank and temporarily suspended business. The reorganization was completed on the 23rd. However, the general ledger has been taken away by Manager Wu. The bank has resumed business as usual on the 24th. All fixed-term deposits and zero-deposit installments can only be paid after they expire. The savings department and current accounts will be paid as usual. The bank's staff has also been changed.

Female Corpse Found Shot in Xinfeng Village

On the morning of the day before yesterday, a female corpse shot to death was suddenly found next to the road in Shenzhuang Village, Xinfeng District, Jiaxing. The local police reported it to the local sub-court for inspection. It was verified that the deceased was shot to death during her lifetime, and it was also found that the corpse was Zhu Erbao, from Pinghu. It is unknown why she was murdered here. After the corpse's mother, Zhu Wu, identified the corpse, she filed a petition with the court to arrest the murderer and punish them, as her daughter was shot to death and it was premeditated, and she died so tragically.

Pinghu

Major Battle Between Tax Police and Salt Smugglers

Most of the residents along the coast of this county and Haiyan County live by selling salt. As the autumn harvest is hopeless this year, they gathered in large groups to load salt for export. The captain of the Changchuan Dam tax police team, Hong Yishan, heard about it and sent seven soldiers to block the Ma'anshan pass. As expected, more than 300 salt smugglers were found in groups passing through the area. Knowing that they were no match, the soldiers let them pass. When there were about thirty or fifty burdens left, they fired blank shots to try to intercept the tail salt. When the salt smugglers heard the gunshots, they immediately returned, each holding sharp knives and carrying poles, surrounding the mountain and wanting to get the soldiers to be satisfied. The soldiers fired more than 100 shots in a chaotic manner, but it was still difficult to escape the danger. At this time, the sound of gunshots was faintly heard from Changchuan Dam. Captain Hong knew that something had happened and immediately transferred the nearby team and negotiated with the army units stationed at the dam for assistance. They rushed to rescue the soldiers. One salt smuggler and one woman from a nearby residence were killed, two people were captured alive, and more than 40 burdens of smuggled salt were taken back to the team. Before the deployment was completed, a report was suddenly received that the salt smugglers vowed not to give up and had gathered in a certain place, threatening to counterattack the team headquarters. The residents of Changchuan Dam were afraid that the entire town would be ruined and had sent several representatives to persuade the salt smugglers, seeking a peaceful solution, but no confirmation had been received as of press time.

Yangzhou

Transportation Envoy Borrows Money to Build Salt Warehouses on Four Banks

The dispute over the Twelve Wharf sail transport has been brewing for years and has not been completely resolved. According to news from the Salt Affairs Department, Transportation Envoy Miao had long drafted a plan. After the sail transport at the Twelve Wharf is cancelled, the ships will directly arrive at the four banks. The locations of the salt warehouses on the four banks have also been selected, including (1) three locations on the Xiang bank, Yuezhou, Changsha, and Hengyang; (2) two locations on the E bank, Hankou and Xindi; (3) two locations on the Xi bank, Jiujiang and Zhongxing; (4) two locations on the Wan bank, Datong and Wuhu. For the salt warehouse expenses, a loan of ten million has been taken from the Shanghai Banking Group, with sixty percent used for building warehouses and forty percent used for handling the Twelve Wharf construction, and for building bundles of bagged salt hemp bags.

Shanghai Bank Establishes Jiangbei District Branch

Shanghai Bank has a branch in Yangzhou. In order to expand its business and centralize Jiangbei finance, it plans to expand the branch into a Jiangbei District Branch. Cai Yunxun, the manager of the Zhenjiang Branch, has been decided to be appointed as the manager. The head office has now drafted this plan in detail and it will be implemented at the end of this year. At that time, the bank building will still need to be rebuilt.

Ningbo

Floating Fire at Pier Causes Fatality

The Hongxing Shipping Company on Binjiang Road in this port held a fire-releasing ceremony at its pier at 7 pm last night (22nd) according to custom. For a time, gongs and drums were loud, and pedestrians flocked to the event. Ni, the wife of the lacquerer Sha Dulai, who lived at the Shizi Well Intersection, also went to watch the event at about 8 pm with her daughter, Ensi. Because there were mountains of people watching, the mother and daughter stood on the small pier. Ensi was small and could not see the whole picture, so she crossed from the small pier to the big pier. However, because the distance was about one foot and the child was weak, she accidentally lost her footing and fell into the water, drifting away with the tide. By the time her mother noticed and called for help, she was gone. At this time, Ni was heartbroken and tried to commit suicide by throwing herself into the water. Fortunately, she was rescued by onlookers and did not drown. After the incident, the patrol police at the scene took Ni to the bureau, ordered the monks to stop chanting, and took the bookkeeper of the Hongxing Shipping Company, Geng Zhiqing, to the bureau for questioning. He was temporarily released on bail to await summons. What happens next, please wait for a follow-up report.

Major Fire on Baizhang Road, Jiangdong

The Hengchangxiang Nanhuo Shop at No. 36 Baizhang Road, Jiangdong, in this port suddenly caught fire downstairs at about 11 pm last night (22nd). For a time, the fire was fierce and unapproachable. It was not until after 12 o'clock that it was extinguished. The victims included Yuanshun Butcher Shop, Cuisheng Paper Shop, Ganhe Salted Goods Shop, Xiangmao Fruit Shop, Yanchunyuan Restaurant, Wang Dexing Secondhand Shop, Jishantang Pharmacy, Daiyuanxing and Xin Dasheng Iron Shops, Lu Yinhua Eye Clinic, and many residents. More than thirty houses were burned down, and the loss reached about 100,000 yuan. Zhang Yousheng, a 15-year-old apprentice at the Hengchangxiang Nanhuo Shop, suddenly disappeared after the fire broke out. It is feared that he was too young to escape and was buried in the fire.

Local News

Seven Months of National Foreign Trade

Imports Exceed Exports by Over 320 Million Yuan

Exports and Imports Decrease Compared to the Same Period Last Year

The Shenshi News Agency reports that the Jianghai Customs announced yesterday that the national trade deficit from January to July this year reached over 322.9 million yuan. The national trade deficit for July alone was over 28.6 million yuan. Both exports and imports have sharply decreased compared to the same period last year and the previous month. The details are as follows:

(Trade Deficit Exceeds 300 Million) From January to July this year, the cumulative total of national foreign trade imports was 643,378,879 yuan, and the cumulative total of exports was 313,458,855 yuan, resulting in a trade deficit of 329,920,024 yuan. The total imports this year decreased by 230,978,413 yuan compared to 874,357,292 yuan in the same period last year. The total exports decreased by 45,560,547 yuan compared to 359,019,402 yuan in the same period last year. The total value of national imports in July was 73,529,043 yuan, a decrease of 29,720,164 yuan compared to the same period last year and a decrease of 12,730,370 yuan compared to June. The total value of exports was 44,914,141 yuan, a decrease of 17,638,742 yuan compared to the same period last year and a decrease of 4,258,655 yuan compared to June.

(Major Import Values) The major import values for the country in July were: various cotton cloths, 584,142 yuan; cotton, 3,643,925 yuan; woolen fabrics, 1,564,742 yuan; rayon, 81,093 yuan; metals, 4,018,005 yuan; machinery, 2,721,646 yuan; automobiles, 520,700 yuan; metal products, 2,103,206 yuan; rice, 1,916,451 yuan; sugar, 1,248,301 yuan; tobacco, 1,371,401 yuan; chemicals, 1,792,670 yuan; dyes, 1,809,364 yuan; gasoline, 319,684 yuan; kerosene, 242,411 yuan; paper, 1,905,740 yuan; timber, 1,261,744 yuan; coal, 353,829 yuan; rubber and its products, 541,501 yuan; lubricating oil, 234,449 yuan (The above are all in Customs Gold Units, each unit approximately equal to 1.995 National Currency yuan).

(Major Export Values) The major export values for the country in July were: pig bristles, 1,457,828 yuan; eggs and egg products, 4,872,812 yuan; pig intestines, 515.25 yuan; raw and processed leather and leather goods, 1,094,8016 yuan; soybeans, 776,363 yuan; miscellaneous grains and their products, 1,120,418 yuan; tung oil, 2,792,242 yuan; seeds, 2,427,778 yuan; tea, 5,390,222 yuan; tobacco, 534,719 yuan; coal, 507,952 yuan; paper, 501,746 yuan; silk, 2,379,059 yuan; cotton yarn, 1,883,619 yuan; various silk fabrics, 2,340,067 yuan; woolen carpets, 437,370 yuan; tungsten ore, 1,043,933 yuan; antimony, 347,027 yuan; tin ingots, 293,584 yuan; straw hat braids, 217,123 yuan; various mats, 442,098 yuan; cotton, 762,363 yuan; ramie, 501,644 yuan; wool, 750,944 yuan (The above are all in National Currency units).

The Situation Between Japan and Russia Becomes Increasingly Urgent

U.S. Warship Sails from Qingdao to Shanghai

Japanese Warships Sail to Dalian

Planes Sent to Harbin

The Greater American Daily News reports that the U.S. naval flagship Augusta, under urgent orders, sailed from Qingdao to Shanghai this afternoon and is expected to arrive tomorrow, followed by two destroyers. However, this information has not been verified by official sources. Unverified news received in Shanghai this morning from Manchuria claims that the Japanese government has dispatched 30 warships to Dalian and 70 bomber planes to Harbin. It is believed that these actions are closely related to the stalemate in negotiations between Russia and "Manchukuo" regarding the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, which has led to a tense situation. When inquired about this matter at the Japanese consulate this morning, a spokesperson replied that the statement may be partially true because the Japanese army and navy are currently conducting large-scale maneuvers in the Dalian and Shanhaiguan areas. Airplanes would naturally participate in large-scale army and navy maneuvers. However, the spokesperson denied that the actions of the warships and airplanes had any connection with the tense situation between Russia and "Manchukuo," stating that neither Japan nor Russia is preparing for war. The spokesperson also mentioned the discord between Russia and Japan, stating that Japanese authorities discovered on August 13th and 14th a conspiracy by a five-member Soviet Russian military delegation to attack the office of the Japanese military delegation at that location. The Japanese and "Manchukuo" newspapers have given this matter extensive coverage, and the Soviet Russian government has not denied it, as it usually does. Furthermore, the "Manchukuo" authorities arrested Soviet Russian employees of the Chinese Eastern Railway for colluding with bandits to destroy Japanese trains transporting soldiers and military supplies, and the Soviet Russian government has not protested. The silence of the Soviet Russian government on both cases is sufficient proof that it is aware of its own wrongdoing.

Commemoration of Confucius' Birthday

Central Government Orders Factories to Close

Local Party and Government Actively Preparing

The Guomin News Agency reports that the 27th of this month is the anniversary of the birth of Confucius. The central government has already passed a resolution designating it as a national memorial day. Upon receiving the order, the local party and government organizations immediately began joint preparations and decided to hold a commemorative meeting at 10:00 AM on that day in the Great Hall of the People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road. All agencies, organizations, and factories in the city will be closed for one day. In addition to sending one representative to participate in the commemorative meeting, all schools will hold separate ceremonies to commemorate the event. The details are as follows:

Proposed List of Officials for the General Assembly

The presidium of the commemorative meeting is planned to have seven members: (1) Tong Xingbai of the Municipal Party Headquarters; (2) Wu Tiecheng of the Municipal Government; (3) Yang Hu of the Municipal Security Bureau; (4) Tao Baichuan of the Municipal Education Association; (5) Yu Zuoting of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; (6) Zhu Xuefan of the Municipal General Labor Union; (7) Yu Zhenhui of the Municipal Farmers' Association. Recorder: Tong Muge. Master of ceremonies: Zhang Hanyun. The Municipal Government will be responsible for hospitality. The Publicity and Investigation Sections of the Municipal Party Headquarters will be responsible for security. The Municipal Police Bureau will send a military band to provide music and dispatch police to maintain order at the venue.

(Schools Commemorate Separately) All major and minor schools in the city regard Confucius as the founder of our country's education system. The memorial measures prescribed by the Central Government should be grand ceremonies to show respect. In addition to sending representatives to participate in the commemorative meeting of party and government organs, they will also hold separate ceremonies at the same time, reporting on Confucius's actions of diligence and love of learning, and hoisting flags for a day off to celebrate. Because the time is approaching and it is also the start of the school year, preparations are very busy.

(Telegram Orders Factories to Close) Although the Central Government has designated this Confucius' birthday as a national memorial day, the Municipal Party Department of this city believes that there are no explicit regulations on whether all factories in the country should be closed. Therefore, it telegraphed the Central Government for instructions a few days ago. It is heard that the department received a reply from the Central Government last night, stating briefly that for the Confucius' birthday memorial, the Central Government has decided that all agencies, organizations, and schools will be closed on this day, and factories should be no exception. After receiving the order, the department immediately notified the relevant organizations and factories throughout the city that they should follow the usual national memorial day procedures and close for one day.

Yesterday Was the Hottest Day After Autumn

Highest Temperature Reached 100 Degrees

Hurricane Lingers and Does Not Advance

The Guowen News Agency reports that the climate in Shanghai has been unusually hot this summer, with no rainfall, causing damage to agriculture and creating a disaster. The general public originally hoped that the arrival of autumn would bring some relief from the intense heat. However, since the beginning of autumn, not only has there been no rain, but the temperature has remained high. As a result, the hopes for a partial autumn harvest in the surrounding countryside are fading away. The reporter inquired at the Shanghai Observatory yesterday and was told that yesterday's temperature was the hottest in recent days, with a maximum of 100 degrees Fahrenheit and a minimum of 76.1 degrees Fahrenheit. There were no clouds in the sky, and the air pressure was not low, so there were no signs of rain. As for the hurricane in the Pacific Ocean, it continues to blow towards the coast of China, which may bring cooler temperatures in the near future. However, according to a report received at 6:00 AM yesterday, the hurricane had blown to 18 degrees North latitude and 131 degrees East longitude, with the wind direction being northwest. However, a report received at 2:00 PM stated that it had stalled. Furthermore, it was found that the hurricane's force was not very strong, so it is not possible to predict whether the wind will blow to the coast and whether the temperature will cool down within days.

It is Said That Kong Xiangxi Will Convene Another Silver Meeting

Bankers Deny It

Believe There Is No Need to Hold a Meeting

The Guowen News Agency reports that yesterday there were rumors that Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi was convening another silver meeting in Guling, and that bankers were rushing to Lushan. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency specifically visited the banking community yesterday to inquire about the situation, and all denied that this was the case. Furthermore, Xu Kan, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, has not left Shanghai, which further proves that the rumors are untrue. According to a certain important person, the government is unwilling to take any action on this matter, as it would only cause more suspicion. Therefore, there is absolutely no plan to convene another meeting of bankers, and there is no need to hold a meeting. It is quite troublesome to investigate whether there is silver being exported every day and how much. However, the more silver that is exported, the tighter the silver supply in the country becomes. The extent of the tightness of the silver supply can be seen from the amount of the silver discount. It is said that when the tide rises, the boat also rises. Before the rural economy was concentrated in the cities, the Shanghai silver dollar discount was above one jiao. Since the rural economy has collapsed and silver has gradually concentrated in the cities, Shanghai has had a surplus of silver, and the silver discount has also decreased accordingly. The Money Industry Association had a record of a minimum interest rate of four fen in June and July of this year. Yesterday, it had risen to one jiao and five fen. The process was roughly: on August 1, the silver discount was seven fen, on the 17th the discount was eight fen, on the 20th it had risen to one jiao, on the 21st it was one jiao and one fen, on the 22nd it was one jiao and three fen, and on the 24th (yesterday) it was one jiao and five fen. It is heard that the money industry has set a limit of no more than seven jiao for the discount, but during the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the silver discount once rose to more than eight jiao.

Yu Shun Expected to Arrive Today

Smooth Sailing Allowed for Quick Arrival

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yu Shun steamer lost its propeller in the waters off Fuzhou. The company dispatched the Wu Yang steamer to tow it. It was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on Sunday morning. At noon yesterday, the company received a follow-up telegram from the Yu Shun stating that after the Wu Yang steamer towed it from Matsu, the journey had been smooth and the speed had been increased, so it was expected to be towed to Wusong on the afternoon of the 25th. After arriving in Wusong, it is planned to detach the Yu Shun and proceed to port first. The company will send another small steamer to tow the Yu Shun into the Huangpu River outside the port of Wusong, stop at the South Wharf, and transfer the cargo from each hold to the Wu Yang before entering the factory for repairs. None of the cargo on board was damaged. The company has informed all cargo owners and insurance companies.

Depression in Yangtze River Shipping

Foreign Ships Manipulate Freight Rates

Chinese Merchants Are Greatly Threatened

Combined Transport Cannot Be Realized

The Yangtze River route has always been the best route for various shipping companies, with the most cargo transported up and down the river. The six companies operating on the route used to be profitable every year, but this year, the volume of cargo traveling up and down the river has plummeted. In addition, the Land and River Navigation Bureau is handling combined land and water transport, so foreign merchant ships on the route, in order to prepare for the worst, have drastically lowered freight rates in an attempt to undermine the situation, leading to the current state of extreme depression in the Yangtze River shipping business and hindering the realization of the Pinghan combined transport. This matter is closely related to the shipping industry, so the current situation is reported as follows:

Few Goods, Many Ships Currently, there are six companies operating on the Yangtze River route: China Merchants, Sanbei, Ning Shao, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Nisshin Kisen. The number of ships operating has decreased by five or six compared to before the January 28th Incident (referring to the Shanghai-Hankou section). For cargo traveling upstream from Shanghai to Hankou, the six companies still maintain the same pace and are not allowed to increase or decrease rates without authorization. However, the freight rates for cargo traveling downstream from Hankou can be increased or decreased independently. This year, due to the impact of the depressed market, the volume of cargo traveling up and down the Yangtze River has decreased significantly. Some ships have only been loaded to 30-40% of their capacity, so the feeling is that there are many ships and few goods. Jardine Matheson intends to sell its Lianhe ship, and Nisshin Kisen has repeatedly wanted to restore its four ships that have been suspended for a long time, but has stopped due to a lack of cargo to transport. The China Merchants' plan to add two Jianglun ships has also been shelved.

Foreign Ships Lower Prices Since the China Merchants and Pinghan Railway reached an 18-article draft agreement on combined land and water transport in March of this year, it has been five months, and it has been said that it will be implemented, but it has not yet been realized. However, since this incident occurred, foreign merchant ships operating on the Yangtze River, such as Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Nisshin Kisen, have been deeply concerned that they will be severely hit after implementation, as all downstream cargo will be converted to combined transport. Therefore, without waiting for its implementation, they have repeatedly reduced the freight rates for cargo transported from the Yangtze River to Shanghai and for cargo transferred from the Yangtze River to Xiamen and Guangdong, not just once. So far, there have even been cases where the downstream cargo freight rates have been reduced to only 30% of the original price. The foreign merchants' intention is that rather than letting the ships travel empty, they would rather lower the freight rates and load the ships, which has led to a disruption of the freight rates. Chinese ships feel threatened by this, and no trip up or down the river is without losses, leading to an unprecedented situation on the Yangtze River for decades.

Each Ship Loses Money This year, none of the Yangtze River ships of any company can make a profit. Foreign companies have accumulated vast wealth and reserves over the years and have already budgeted for losses. Chinese shipping lines are suffering from this blow and are finding it difficult to sustain themselves. Currently, according to precise calculations, the various expenses for a round trip of a ship for ten days are at least 7,000 yuan, while the average income from cargo and passengers traveling up and down the river is at most 5,000 yuan. Therefore, each trip loses between 1,000 and 2,000 yuan. Therefore, Chinese shipping lines urgently need the combined transport to be implemented as soon as possible to save the situation.

Hinders Combined Transport Although the Pinghan combined transport is about to be completed by both the railway and shipping sides, the most difficult point is the freight rate. According to Article 5 of the contract, the combined transport freight rate is determined according to the lowest rate of each shipping company. However, the foreign shipping lines have already lowered their rates to below cost, making it impossible to determine the combined transport freight rate to date. If the current prices are charged, both the railway and shipping sides will lose money. Therefore, the railway and shipping authorities are hesitating greatly. According to Zhou Fengtu, who is in charge of the combined transport, it is difficult to say whether the Pinghan Railway combined transport can be realized on September 15th. If the freight rate problem is not resolved, this matter cannot be discussed at all. According to Zhou, it will probably be difficult to start in mid-September. The issue of Sanbei and Ning Shao sending ships is still under discussion.

Sichuan Fellow Provincial Association

Held a Meeting Yesterday to Discuss the Use of Foreign Capital

The Principle of Using Foreign Capital to Develop Industries Was Approved

A Treaty Research Committee Was Formed to Study the Documents Signed by Both Sides

The Sichuan Fellow Provincial Association in Shanghai, in response to the Juxingcheng Bank's use of foreign capital to develop industries in Sichuan Province, held an executive committee meeting at its office on Shandong Road at 2:00 PM yesterday. More than a dozen people attended, including Tang Zhonghou, Wu Guoliang, Liu Xueqiao, Li Xunfu, Zhong Hangsu, Li Chongpu, Wu Youdan, Qiu Zhizhong, Yu Yuanhui, Deng Youguang, and Tan Jiqing. Li Xunfu chaired the meeting, and Wu Guoliang recorded the proceedings. After the formal opening, the chairman reported on the situation of Juxingcheng's use of foreign capital, and executive committee member Yu Yuanhui, who is also the deputy manager of the bank, reported on the five points of the process (the same as the five points reported in the newspaper, so they are omitted). The discussion of each case then began as follows: (1) How should this association express its opinion on the Juxing Bank's use of foreign capital? (Resolution) A. Under the conditions of using foreign capital to develop industries in Sichuan Province without harming sovereignty, the Juxing Bank's use of foreign capital is approved. B. This association will form a treaty research committee, appointing Zhong Hangsu, Li Xunfu, Qiu Zhizhong, Wu Youdan, Liu Xueqiao, Li Chongpu, Deng Youguang, and seven others as members, and designating Zhong Hangsu to convene the committee. C. The Juxingcheng Bank will be requested by letter to send all documents related to this matter to this association, and the special committee will study them. (2) What should be done about the telegram from Liu Xiang, the Director of Sichuan Post-Disaster Relief, requesting assistance due to the severe drought and flood situation? (Resolution) A. A telegram will be sent to the government requesting the allocation of funds for disaster relief. B. A reply will be sent to Director Liu Xiang. (3) Committee members Liu Xueqiao, Tang Zhonghou, and Qiu Zhizhong requested that the association's public welfare committee member Yin Daoxin be sent back to Sichuan to investigate the economic situation and industrial conditions. (Resolution) Passed. Other cases were omitted. The meeting adjourned at around 5:00 PM.

Today There Are

4.7 Million Silver Dollars Being Shipped to America

Loaded onto the British Steamer Sun Bound for New York

The Total Exceeds 10 Million in Nine Batches

36 million silver dollars were just loaded and exported by various foreign banks three days ago. Yesterday afternoon, various foreign banks reported loading another large batch of silver dollars, totaling 4.7 million yuan, consisting of a mix of large silver bars, silver coins, and foreign currency. They contacted the British firm Jardine Matheson, which loaded the cargo onto its express steamer Sun, bound for New York. The cargo was transferred onto the ship in the afternoon. First, it was transported by truck to the New Customs Wharf, and then transferred to the Sun by barge, where it was hoisted into the silver storage. It will leave Shanghai this morning and is expected to arrive in New York in 34 days. This is the ninth batch of silver dollars being exported. It is said that there will be a tenth batch that will need to be shipped within the week. Since May, a total of nine batches of silver dollars have been shipped from Shanghai to foreign countries, totaling over 100 million yuan.

Page 13

Prolonged Drought Causes Rice Prices to Continue to Rise

The Social Affairs Bureau Plans to Reconsider Rice Price Controls

The drought in the interior has worsened in recent days, causing grain and rice prices to skyrocket and shipments to be scarce. Rice prices in Shanghai have also risen. It is said that the Social Affairs Bureau has sent personnel to investigate and will convene another meeting to discuss rice price controls. The details are as follows:

Jiangbei Bumper Harvest This year, the rice production in areas such as Rugao, Tongzhou, Huai'an, Gaoyou, Shaobo, and Dongtai in Jiangsu Province has been very abundant, and prices are low. As a result, rice merchants from various places are rushing to purchase, causing prices to rise. In recent weeks, the drought in areas such as Wuxi, Suzhou, Pingwang, Tongli, and Changshu has worsened, and the rivers have dried up, causing the rice to wither. As a result, people are panicking and hoarding food, and grain prices have risen from 5.7 yuan to 6.5 yuan per shi. Two shi of grain are equivalent to one shi of rice, and it costs 14 yuan to transport top-grade rice to Shanghai. Shipments are also not strong.

Sending Personnel to Investigate In order to stabilize rice prices, the Social Affairs Bureau previously convened rice industry groups to agree on a maximum price of no more than 13 yuan. However, at that time, people were panicking, so although the surface price was 13 yuan, the actual price was above 13 yuan, with the highest reaching 13.8 yuan and the lowest being 13.4 yuan. Now that rice prices in the interior have risen, the controlled price of 13 yuan is no longer enough to cover the cost by more than one yuan. Therefore, rice merchants are also very panicked and have repeatedly requested the Social Affairs Bureau to revise the price. The Social Affairs Bureau sent Zhou Minggang, a staff member of the Fourth Section, to investigate the north and south markets yesterday morning and is said to be planning to hold a meeting on the 28th to discuss the matter.

Rice Prices Continue to Rise According to Jiang Shizhi, Chairman of the Rice and Grain Merchants Association, when the authorities controlled prices, Saigon rice was selling for only 10 yuan per 200 pounds, but now it has risen to 12 yuan. The price of 8.5 yuan per dan for guest xian rice has already risen to 11 yuan. Currently, top-grade zheng white rice is in short supply, and second-grade rice is selling for 13.3 yuan. First and second-grade japonica rice is selling for 12.8 yuan. The government's prestige should be maintained, but the facts must also be considered. The current price increase is due to the lack of rain.

Zhejiang Plans Relief After purchasing 100,000 shi of Hunan Wuhu japonica and small Jiaomi rice from Shanghai, the price of rice in Zhejiang Province remained high. Therefore, the local rice industry is still continuing to purchase from Shanghai. An average of about 5,000 bags are transported from Shanghai to Hangzhou every day. As of yesterday, 200,000 bags of Shanghai rice have been transported to Zhejiang, and purchases and transport are still being made every day. Recently, the Shanghai rice industry has been entrusted to order 100,000 bags of forward rice from Saigon, with delivery scheduled for next month in Zhejiang.

Zhangzhou Rice Is Suspicious As for the Zhangzhou rice shipment to Shanghai, which various circles suspect, according to people in the rice industry, Tokyo's round-grain japonica rice and Dujian rice are similar to the japonica and Jian rice of Jiangsu Province in our country, making it difficult to distinguish them. It is not easy for those who are not familiar with this industry to distinguish them. Taiwan and Zhangzhou have never had rice come to Shanghai, so it is difficult to imagine what it looks like. However, it is also easy to distinguish between new rice and old rice, because new rice is green in color and tender and soft, and it is easy to break when crushed by hand. Old rice is pure in color, dry and hard, and not easy to crush.

Legislative Member Huang Youchang

Drafted the Commercial Registration Law

Returned to Nanjing from Putuo via Shanghai

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Commercial Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan previously appointed member Huang Youchang to draft the Commercial Registration Law. Huang came to Shanghai to investigate commercial practices with the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce and the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and to solicit opinions on remedial measures for joint and several liability in partnership businesses. After completing the investigation, Huang went to Putuo to draft the registration law. Now that the draft has been completed, Huang returned to Shanghai from Putuo the day before yesterday and went to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for a more detailed discussion. The Chamber of Commerce also had standing committee members Chen Zheqing and Ke Ganchen, and supervisory committee members Fang Jiaobo and Fei Yunqing, contribute as much as possible. Huang has already returned to Nanjing from Shanghai yesterday and will submit the draft for discussion as soon as the Legislative Yuan's recess is over.

The Glory of Domestic Goods Sold in Europe

Calcium Carbonate Produced by Zhaoxin Chemical Factory

The Zhaoxin Chemical Factory, located at Jinjiazhai, West Zhoujiaqiao, West Shanghai, has been in operation since last year. Its chemical raw materials, such as calcium carbonate and magnesium carbonate, are well-received by domestic rubber factories and cosmetics factories. Recently, a major company in Hamburg, Germany, recognizing the factory's superior products, specifically ordered a large quantity of calcium carbonate from the factory for shipment to Germany for distribution. This is truly a pioneering achievement for domestic raw materials being sold overseas. It is reported that the factory plans to greatly expand its product range this year, including more than ten types such as oxalic acid, sodium sulfate, potassium carbonate, liver of sulfur, descaling powder, silver polishing powder, yellow and white essence, and dextrin. All are important raw materials for the chemical industry. Its various medicinal products are especially welcomed by major pharmacies, which are placing orders in a rush, creating a situation where the factory is overwhelmed with demand.
