Using Red Zinc Ore to Make an Amplifier-Stage Crystal Radio

— Ying Fu

Ordinary amplification work is done with vacuum tubes, which is something everyone knows, but if you are limited by economy, then it is not impossible to use red zinc ore (Zincite) instead.

Red zinc ore is a natural zinc oxide, its chemical symbol is ZnO, and like galena, it has the ability to detect waves, but it has not been widely adopted for detection because it requires electricity. If it is in contact with a metal, such as steel, or carbon, it can generate alternating current of various frequencies, so under certain combinations, its working condition is very similar to a triode. Russian engineer Rosov once invented using it to make an amplifier.

The following crystal radio is based on Rosov's theory. The results are very good. In this city, it can be used with a small loudspeaker to listen to major radio stations, and it is a bit deafening to listen with headphones. However, powerful loudspeakers cannot be used, because the characteristic is not linear, so it will be very distorted.

The circuit is also very simple, but it is a crystal radio with excellent selectivity, plus a stage of red zinc ore low amplification.

(ZnO) is red zinc ore, first insert a steel nail into a tube, then place it in the ore pan, and then wrap it with a piece of flannel, connect the positive pole to one end of the red zinc ore, and the negative pole to one end of the steel nail.

L uses No. 26 silk-covered wire to wind twenty turns on a small spider web board, and L2 uses the same number wire to wind fifty turns on a large spider web board. After winding, it can be installed on a push-pull frame.

C is a 0.0003 microfarad variable capacitor.

C1, C2 are 0.0001 microfarad variable capacitors.

C3, C4 are 0.002 microfarad fixed capacitors.

D is ordinary crystal, but the quality must be good.

R is a 300 ohm fixed resistor.

R1 is a 1500 ohm variable resistor.

A 40 or 45 volt B battery can be used for the dry battery.

I must mention in passing is the problem of the antenna and ground wire, which must be installed well here. The height of the antenna should be 10 meters, and it is best to use two 40-meter-long ones, in a parallel style, the distance between the style lines is about 1 meter, and the lead-in line is a T-style. The ground wire should be as short as possible, and if it is wrapped around a tap water pipe, it must be wrapped tightly.

Partitioning

— Hu Wen'an

In radio, partitioning is used to prevent electrical energy from being transmitted between two circuits. We generally use lead as the best material for partitioning because it has low electrical resistance and is extremely light.

But why is partitioning so necessary? Because any circuit containing alternating current emits a magnetic field and an electrostatic field. The higher the alternating current frequency, the greater the ability to radiate. Therefore, this phenomenon is even more pronounced in radio high-frequency situations. Within a radio receiver, any conductor carrying this frequency of current radiates its energy at any time, causing surrounding conductors to receive it and generating unwanted interference, feedback, and other undesirable results within the receiver.

To avoid the above situation, a large piece of conductor is often placed around high-frequency circuits as a partition. This allows it to absorb the electrical energy released by the former, generating eddy currents and dissipating them in the partition. The consumption of electrical energy can be calculated according to Ohm's law: I² × R. However, at the same time, because current is generated in this partition, it opposes the original circuit, reducing its radiation and lowering the loss of electrical energy. Moreover, the partition's inductive capacity is directly proportional to its current I. Therefore, manufacturers often use thicker partitions to obtain a smaller R value and increase the I value, thus improving the effectiveness of the partition.

In addition to high-frequency amplification, intermediate-frequency amplification tubes, oscillating tubes, and their regulating coils and capacitors must be individually partitioned. The wiring between them should also be partitioned with flexible copper wire tubes.

Partitioning can isolate magnetic fields and separate electrostatic potentials. How is this done? By directly grounding the partition. This assumes that the ground is a permanent neutralizer.

Since the partition absorbs electrical energy, it should be as far away from the object being partitioned as possible within a feasible range. It must also be noted that this partition absolutely cannot be used to conduct any kind of circuit, otherwise, it will lose its original purpose. Therefore, the grounding of the high-frequency circuit wiring in the radio receiver must be gathered in one place and not connected to the chassis at any time, so that the chassis, which has the mission of partitioning, can also serve as a conductor of high-frequency current.

Using Old Vacuum Tubes as Lightning Arresters

— Gu Weiyou

Now that the weather is hot, the most feared thing for radios is lightning. If a radio is not equipped with a lightning arrester, there is a risk of it being destroyed by lightning. However, buying a lightning arrester is not cheap. There is a type of carbon resistor lightning arrester, which can only be used once and must be repurchased, which is not economical. For comrades who study radio, there must be vacuum tubes with burned filaments in the laboratory. Now, use them to make a vacuum-type lightning arrester. When the antenna receives high-voltage lightning, it passes through the lead-in wire to the plate of the old vacuum tube and flies to the grid to the ground, becoming a short circuit. It no longer passes through other parts of the radio, so the radio is safe. Moreover, it can still be used after a lightning strike. The connection method is to connect a wire from the antenna terminal to the plate of the old vacuum tube, and then use another wire to connect one end of the ground terminal to the grid of the old vacuum tube. In this way, a lightning arrester is successfully made. The attached diagram is above:

Simple Lightning Arrester

— Xu Xiyu

Although this summer is extraordinarily hot, with the scorching sun in the sky and no cool air at all, and the dark clouds have disappeared to who knows where, experience tells us that rain is coming, and the sounds of thunder and lightning will constantly appear in the sky, because this is the so-called season of "continuous autumn rains"!

Isn't it true that those who have radios—with antennas—will suffer at that time? At best, the radio will be damaged; at worst, a fire will be caused.

According to theory, since the antenna of a radio can receive radio waves, needless to say, it must be able to induce atmospheric electricity.

Therefore, if you already have a lightning arrester installed, that's best! If not, please find a way to install one immediately!

The simplest way is to go to a radio supply store and buy one, but it will cost at least one or two yuan to five or six yuan!

Here is an extremely economical, simple, and excellent lightning arrester, which is the result of the author's experience, and its performance is no less than that of ready-made ones on the market.

Find two sections of useless—used-up—small dry batteries, and try to peel off the zinc skin that wraps around them, and then you can see the carbon rod inside. Be careful not to break it when taking it out. Also, prepare a piece of plastic board three inches long and one and a half inches wide, and two wiring nails.

Connect one end of each carbon rod with copper wire, as shown in the diagram.

Radio

In the diagram, only one antenna is used to receive the radio, because if the ground wire is also connected like the antenna, then the lightning arrester will be completely ineffective during lightning. If the reader's radio requires the ground wire to be directly connected to the radio, then you might as well install another one, because this ground wire is only for the lightning arrester and has nothing to do with the radio.

As for the distance between the carbon rods, it must be between one and two points. Do not connect them!

Supplement to the Shanghai Newspaper

Essays

Scientific Disaster

— Zhaozhao

The other day, another tragic accident occurred in a factory in Shanghai. Before that, there had been multiple boiler explosions in factories, killing and injuring as many as three or four hundred people, and as few as dozens. If anyone were to survey such a disaster site, squeezing in from among the nearby onlookers and the cries of families helping the old and the young, they would see broken walls and collapsed houses, with lingering smoke everywhere. Many rescuers would be dragging out sections of mutilated limbs amidst the pungent, acrid, and fishy odor. Some were already burned into the shape of a bow, others were like charcoal-mixed roast beef, a blur with no way to identify their faces. It was truly a living hell, terrifying and heartbreaking.

According to statistics from the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, from the 16th to the 21st year of the Republic of China, there were a total of 319 factory disasters in the public concession in six years, with a total loss of more than 1.56 million taels of silver. The French concession and the Chinese area were not included. Last year alone, there were 165 industrial disasters in Shanghai, according to newspaper reports, with more than 410 deaths and injuries and losses of more than 2.3 million yuan. In January and February of this year, there were a total of 46 accidents, with 53 deaths and injuries. Most of them were explosions or fires. The number of such disasters is increasing year by year, indicating the neglect of factory safety in all aspects. Although there are many factories in Shanghai, how difficult is it for them to gradually destroy themselves? Men and women who escaped death in the mainland finally had their pitiful lives ended by a mouthful of bitter food!

Originally, when science develops, people's surroundings are full of sharp weapons, and it can also be said that the surroundings are full of dangers. For example, the distribution of urban electricity is as dense as a network, providing transportation, communication, entertainment, cooling, and heating, as well as the passage of coal gas and the supply of steam for power and room temperature, drawbridges, tunnels, high and low cars, trains, dozens of layers of cement buildings... In various forms, each one can lead to a catastrophic disaster if there is no sound scientific method as a basis and insurance.

Then, do so many factories now also have technicians, use science, and do the factory owners and managers not have preventive equipment in advance, or equipment to learn from the disasters of others? If we examine it carefully, we will know that the so-called material science, like politics, law, etc., changes its shape when it comes to China. The result of its implementation is that the weak can be slowly killed, and the strong will immediately give you floods and beasts, causing the country to sink and perish. In short, science becomes a "scientific disaster" when it comes to China.

Let's look at the facts: events such as praying for rain, offering sacrifices, fortune-telling, and automatic writing are still prevalent everywhere in our country. The minds of our nation are still stagnating in a kind of vague influence, an unquestioning metaphysical aspiration, and there is no clear scientific mind above the general level. If you say he is unscientific, he will immediately turn his mind and put a scientific hat on all kinds of old tricks, and then there will be scientific fortune-telling, scientific mediums, etc. Anyway, science is the best in the West. To run a business, just buy one or two sets of "foreign cars" from the red-haired or the Star-Spangled Banner (Shanghai commonly calls machines "cars," and machine managers are called "car managers") and you can use them permanently. The science in schools is just a matter of playing Western tricks by following the examples in the books for a while. What precise observation is there, what accurate understanding is there, and naturally, what experience is there in manipulation. They see foreign factories safe and developed at the same time and place, while they are always catching fire, collapsing, and exploding!

If anyone can go and see the factories of Chinese merchants everywhere, they can see that many factories are simple and crude, with sheds and scaffolding erected haphazardly. Those steel pipes and iron frames are mostly covered with dust and grease, and those brackets and motors make the roof tiles shake. The air in all parts of the factory is turbid, the light is not adjusted, the labor is crowded, and the residual materials are messy. The order is

Page 22

extremely bad. Those factory owners are probably always thinking about how to annex shareholders and become sole proprietors, and the managers are always arranging private affairs, planning to embezzle property, using their positions to benefit themselves. Even if there are a few who shout out the scientific management method, they don't actually understand what science is, but use fashionable slogans to exploit workers and deceive their bosses, with other purposes. The most ridiculous thing is that many of the people who manage factories don't even know the names of the various parts of the machinery, let alone how to use and protect them. They just use a few old foremen from apprentice backgrounds, relying on the experience of the early 19th century, to barely operate the new machinery of the 20th century. They also hire a group of police, constables, old men, and labor scabs, who are densely distributed inside and outside, closing the doors and locking them, and suppressing a group of tame sheep. Once a tragedy occurs, there is no way to escape, and a large number of families die together! Isn't this a scientific disaster?

Scientific disaster! In China, it will cause disasters that others will never cause. And in the world, it has another kind of disaster, that is, artillery, airplanes, tanks, germs, poison gas, and death rays. Countries are exhausting their efforts to research, manufacture, store, and train, preparing to fight for markets and slaughter the poor people of other countries. That is also a kind of scientific disaster, which is not worth mentioning. But today we are too late to mourn their great disaster and we have to blame ourselves for falling and breaking our heads on a flat and walkable road.

The Sudden Death

— Feng

It was just dawning when he woke up. His body was soft and limp all over, and he was very thirsty. He looked at his wife on the ground, sleeping soundly, her mouth open, her sallow, thin face, and her disheveled hair. She had not slept well for three days, so the husband could not bear to wake her. He forced himself to get up, but when his legs crossed the bed, they were shaky and weak. He bent over and staggered to the table, grabbed the teapot and drank it heartily, and his spirits seemed to be revitalized a little.

They were a couple. The husband pulled a rickshaw, and the wife helped people wash clothes, barely living a life of not being able to eat enough to avoid starvation. Naturally, it was much better than being left to die after the flood in their hometown; however, they had heard the old man at the ferry tell stories about Shanghai: gold was paved on the ground, and as long as you had the ability, you could become a rich man from morning to evening, so they traveled thousands of miles to this big city. Now, after a full two years, they had recognized everything and understood everything. Who said this was not a paradise, but how could it not be a hell!

Their life was a life in hell!

Working like cattle and horses, who is made of iron? The husband fell ill, vomiting and diarrhea violently, which is a terminal illness for the poor, because their dictionary does not have the word "medicine."

The wife was so busy that she had not slept well for three days. With one less person making money and one more person eating, the family could not support it no matter what. So she washed clothes day and night, trying to do twice the work of her husband's legs from her wrists.

This is the fate of the poor, and they cannot blame heaven.

The husband knew that his wife was not a strong person, and he did not want to lie down again before he got up, so when he felt a little revitalized, he strenuously swung his legs to make a rickshaw-pulling posture, but it startled his wife on the ground. She rubbed her blurry eyelids and sat up from the ground, asking what the husband was doing.

He lifted his hairy legs and replied with a smile: "I have strength!"

"Rest for another day; I can go collect the money today."

"Isn't it good to earn a little more money when you have nothing to do? You also sleep comfortably for a while today." The husband drank a few more mouthfuls of cold tea and was ready to go out.

"Then come back earlier." She lay down weakly again, not seeing clearly that her husband's legs did not have the same strength as before.

Pulling the empty car slowly, the world seemed to have been separated from him for a long time. The sun had just risen from the east, and it no longer felt as comfortable on his body as it had before he went out, but he received a long-distance business, and he mustered up the courage to run forward.

When he arrived at his destination, beads of sweat the size of soybeans fell down. Panting, he sat on the foot of the car and could no longer stand up. He fell into a daze for more than an hour, and he pulled the empty car home like a snail.

In front of a factory gate, he was called to stop. Several people were helping a man with a drooping head and wanted him to pull him to the Red Cross. He told them that he couldn't pull it, and one person replied:

"Friend, pull him for a trip. If it's any later, I'm afraid he'll be dead." He pointed to the worker in the crook of his arm.

Like God's will, he stopped the car in front of them, helped the patient onto the car, and then ran forward, with several people following behind.

With a divine power, he pulled so fast, not like a person who had been vomiting and diarrhea for three days. A breath of air in his stomach was rising upward. The faster he pulled, the more comfortable he felt. In a few minutes, he arrived at the Red Cross.

He stopped the car, and the worker who had just spoken thanked him with four mao of money and helped the patient inside. He smiled and took the money, felt dizzy, fell to the ground, and white foam poured out of his mouth. His limbs were convulsing, and in less than two minutes, he died stiffly.

Four mao of money was dropped in the center of the street. This is the fate of the poor, and they cannot blame heaven.

Tricked by the Ancients!

— Hong

The New Autumn Countryside

— Juefu

The cool autumn weather, with its high skies and crisp air, has unknowingly descended upon the world.

Autumn is such a lovely and endearing season! It does not have the unbearable heat of summer, the biting cold of winter, or the alternating cold and warmth and intermittent rain of spring, which make people feel uncomfortable and disgusted. Instead, it has cool breezes and bright moons, giving rise to a sense of beauty like that of a paradise.

When this autumn season, "when the weather is cool but not cold," arrives, the countryside, which has always been very tranquil, feels even more lovely in the evenings after the scorching sun has withdrawn its intense flames:

--The weather is so cool, the night sky is so clear and blue, and the gentle breeze blows through the green groves in bursts, emitting a lingering and desolate sound; the sound waves of chirping insects ripple through the woods from time to time, lingering in the ears; clusters of bright stars are deeply embedded in the blue sky and shine, emitting their only light, illuminating the earth; a crescent of thin, bright new moon hangs shyly in a corner of the western sky, as if inquiring about the secrets of the world. At this time, under the dense shade of willow trees and beside the still water of the pond, three or five farmers and farm women, who have been working hard all day, often gather to chat. Among them, the sounds of complaining, "It's hot! It's hot!..." are no longer heard, and the energetic waving of large palm-leaf fans is no longer seen. Moreover, some people who are not very healthy and cannot resist the invasion of the evening breeze have even put on a light jacket over their shoulders, which have been bare for many days.

In such a scene, if you walk out alone into the boundless wilderness, look up at the thin, bright moon and the twinkling stars in the sky; turn around and face the gentle evening breeze that is blowing slowly, letting it flutter your clothes, brush your skirts, and sweep over your long hair, blowing away all the vulgarity in your brain; you really don't know whether you are still living in this bustling world or have already stepped into a misty fairyland!

I love autumn, especially the secluded and gentle early autumn evenings. I wish it would stay in the world forever, allowing the filthy people to be intoxicated in its soft embrace like light smoke and flowing clouds!

Evening

— Yefei

I was alone, carrying a wounded heart, walking, walking on the path at dusk, heading towards my destination - home. The muddy road after the rain was strangely slippery. If I stepped on it, I would accidentally fall into the pond. The autumn insects in the field were mourning with hissing voices; the tone was so miserable. The faint barking of dogs swept past my ears, and a small village was reflected in front of me.

I groped my way home, pushed the door open, and saw that Li Jun was still doing needlework under the kerosene lamp, waiting for me, not sleeping. When she saw me, she looked me up and down with surprised eyes and said:

"Ping! Why are you in such a hurry today! You look very bad! Were you frightened?" As she spoke, she went to get a towel to wipe the cold sweat off me; I didn't answer her, and I felt extremely tired.

"Sigh! Ping! You're too tired! However, I can't share some of your strength. I'm always making you so tired. I'm really sorry for you..."

"Ah! What else is there to say? In order to eat and in order to live, I have to pinch my nose and suffer the turtle's anger! Li Jun! Did Aunt Quan come today? The things I discussed with her, there should be some progress, right?"

"She came once today. It looks like there's still some hope."

I dragged my wounded body, and the whip marks of physical life were aching faintly, aching deeply and thoroughly, but I didn't want her to see it; I forced myself to struggle to the door, but she hurried to catch up and supported me.

Page 23

"Ping! Do you want water to drink? There's some in the room!" At that time, I felt a heat in my heart, and my throat was itchy and strange. A fishy smell rushed up from my throat, followed by two coughs, and finally I vomited a large mouthful of fresh blood. She was so frightened and hurriedly helped me to bed and asked me:

"Ping! Ping! What... what's wrong... with you! Don't... don't scare... scare me to death."

As she spoke, she cried. This made me even more upset. I opened my eyes slightly and waved my hand:

"What are you crying for! I won't die just yet: Quick, I feel very uncomfortable, go get me a glass of salt water, the more salt, the better."

She got a glass of salt water and slowly poured it into me. After I finished drinking a glass of salt water, she asked me if I wanted any more. I just shook my head at her and said, "Li Jun! You go to sleep."

"Why did you suddenly have such a problem today? Did you get hurt from working too hard?"

As Li Jun spoke, she took off the dirty clothes on my body that were covered in mud: But, after taking off my clothes, she found red and purple blood marks on my skin, and some of them were oozing out of those strands of fresh blood!

"Oh! What's this! Ping! Who beat you? It's so heartbreaking! Alas!" I looked at her and smiled miserably: "I need to eat! What can I do? Li Jun."

She stroked my wounds and cried on my body, crying sadly and sorrowfully.

An atmosphere of fear and misery filled the entire room.

"Ping! Your body is like this, I'll ask for a leave for you tomorrow, so you can rest for a few days!"

"Yes, but for poor people like us who eat one day at a time, how can we not work for a day? If we don't work for a day, we won't have food to eat for a day. Now, I can still struggle a little, so I have to go and struggle, unless my eyes are completely closed. Vomiting blood! It's not just one day, to tell you the truth,"

Both of them were silent. The night, the deep night, went deeper and deeper, and the air in this room also went as deep as the night.

Amateur Mailbox

Brother and Sister-in-law's Abuse

— Editor

Mr. Editor:

I have a question about my future and am now especially beseeching you, Mr. Editor, to sacrifice some of your precious time to give me guidance.

I am a lonely and weak woman. My parents had three children: my elder brother, my elder sister, and me. My elder brother is married to his wife, and my elder sister is also married. I am the youngest, currently twenty-one years old. Two years ago, my parents passed away, leaving behind an inheritance of several tens of thousands of dollars, which is entirely managed by my brother and sister-in-law. From then on, I have been in a bitter situation. Alas, I am often abused by them at home, treated like a slave. It is truly beyond the power of words to describe.

I graduated from elementary school in the past. Later, because of serving my parents, I stopped studying for several years. I usually studied on my own. This spring, when various schools were holding entrance examinations, I was determined to seek specialized knowledge. As a result, I was admitted to a specialized school. So, I asked them for tuition fees, but I was immediately refused. I didn't get a single cent. Later, relatives tried to persuade them without success. Unable to think of a solution, I had to borrow money from various relatives to be able to enter school. Time flies like an arrow, and one semester has passed. For the tuition fees for the second semester, my relatives are no longer lending me money. I foresee that I will drop out of school again. Now I raise a few points: (1) In such a family situation, should my brother be responsible for providing my tuition fees? (2) If he is not responsible, what should I do? (3) Do women have inheritance rights? (4) How should the inheritance be divided between married and unmarried women? Regarding the above questions, please, Mr. Editor, provide me with detailed instructions in the shortest possible time. I am immensely grateful. Best wishes.

Sincerely, Someone.

Answer: It is indeed an unfortunate thing that you are suffering from the pain inflicted by your brother and sister-in-law. Because among ordinary families, siblings usually have some affection for each other. It is unexpected that your brother and sister-in-law not only do not support your education but also often abuse you, abusing you like a slave. It is truly extraordinary.

However, before answering your questions, there is one point you must pay attention to, which is whether you ultimately have the courage and determination. Because if you do not have the courage and determination, then no matter how much effort is made to answer you, it will be of no avail. Therefore, the most important thing is to see if you yourself can have the courage to do it.

According to the provisions of the laws of the Republic of China, men and women have equal status. Therefore, in the inheritance of property, there is no distinction between importance. Completely according to Article 1141 of the Civil Code, which stipulates that "When there are several heirs of the same order, the inheritance shall be divided equally according to the number of people." In the editor's view, there is no room for compromise between you and your brother and sister-in-law, because they not only abuse you, but even the persuasion of relatives is ineffective. It is conceivable that they are unreasonable. Since your parents had tens of thousands of dollars in inheritance, you can contact your married elder sister to jointly request your brother to divide the inheritance into three parts, because according to Article 1 of the "Detailed Rules for the Implementation of Married Women's Retrospective Inheritance of Property."
